# Psalms

### THE BOOK OF PSALMS

### BOOK I.

## PSALM 1.

Blessed _is_ the man that walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly, nor standeth in the way of sinners, nor sitteth in the seat of the scornful.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>But his delight _is_ in the law of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and in his law doth he meditate day and night.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, that bringeth forth his fruit in his season; his leaf also shall not wither; and whatsoever he doeth shall prosper.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ The ungodly _are_ not so: but _are_ like the chaff which the wind driveth away.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Therefore the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> knoweth the way of the righteous: but the way of the ungodly shall perish.  

## PSALM 2.

Why do the heathen rage, and the people imagine a vain thing?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The kings of the earth set themselves, and the rulers take counsel together, against the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and against his anointed, _saying_,  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let us break their bands asunder, and cast away their cords from us.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He that sitteth in the heavens shall laugh: the Lord shall have them in derision.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Then shall he speak unto them in his wrath, and vex them in his sore displeasure.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Yet have I set my king upon my holy hill of Zion.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ I will declare the decree: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath said unto me, Thou _art_ my Son; this day have I begotten thee.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Ask of me, and I shall give _thee_ the heathen _for_ thine inheritance, and the uttermost parts of the earth _for_ thy possession.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou shalt break them with a rod of iron; thou shalt dash them in pieces like a potter’s vessel.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ Be wise now therefore, O ye kings: be instructed, ye judges of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Serve the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with fear, and rejoice with trembling.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Kiss the Son, lest he be angry, and ye perish _from_ the way, when his wrath is kindled but a little. Blessed _are_ all they that put their trust in him.  

## PSALM 3.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David, when he fled from Absalom his son.</div>

<span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, how are they increased that trouble me! many _are_ they that rise up against me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Many _there be_ which say of my soul, _There is_ no help for him in God. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>But thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _art_ a shield for me; my glory, and the lifter up of mine head.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ I cried unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with my voice, and he heard me out of his holy hill. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I laid me down and slept; I awaked; for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> sustained me.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, that have set _themselves_ against me round about.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Arise, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; save me, O my God: for thou hast smitten all mine enemies _upon_ the cheek bone; thou hast broken the teeth of the ungodly.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Salvation _belongeth_ unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: thy blessing _is_ upon thy people. Selah.  

## PSALM 4.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm of David.</div>

Hear me when I call, O God of my righteousness: thou hast enlarged me _when I was_ in distress; have mercy upon me, and hear my prayer.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>O ye sons of men, how long _will ye turn_ my glory into shame? _how long_ will ye love vanity, _and_ seek after leasing? Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>But know that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath set apart him that is godly for himself: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will hear when I call unto him.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Stand in awe, and sin not: commune with your own heart upon your bed, and be still. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Offer the sacrifices of righteousness, and put your trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ _There be_ many that say, Who will shew us _any_ good? <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, lift thou up the light of thy countenance upon us.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Thou hast put gladness in my heart, more than in the time _that_ their corn and their wine increased.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I will both lay me down in peace, and sleep: for thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, only makest me dwell in safety.  

## PSALM 5.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Nehiloth, A Psalm of David.</div>

Give ear to my words, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, consider my meditation.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Hearken unto the voice of my cry, my King, and my God: for unto thee will I pray.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>My voice shalt thou hear in the morning, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; in the morning will I direct _my prayer_ unto thee, and will look up.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For thou _art_ not a God that hath pleasure in wickedness: neither shall evil dwell with thee.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The foolish shall not stand in thy sight: thou hatest all workers of iniquity.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thou shalt destroy them that speak leasing: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will abhor the bloody and deceitful man.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ But as for me, I will come _into_ thy house in the multitude of thy mercy: _and_ in thy fear will I worship toward thy holy temple.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Lead me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, in thy righteousness because of mine enemies; make thy way straight before my face.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For _there is_ no faithfulness in their mouth; their inward part _is_ very wickedness; their throat _is_ an open sepulchre; they flatter with their tongue.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Destroy thou them, O God; let them fall by their own counsels; cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions; for they have rebelled against thee.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>But let all those that put their trust in thee rejoice: let them ever shout for joy, because thou defendest them: let them also that love thy name be joyful in thee.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>For thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, wilt bless the righteous; with favour wilt thou compass him as _with_ a shield.  

## PSALM 6.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician on Neginoth upon Sheminith, A Psalm of David.</div>

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, rebuke me not in thine anger, neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Have mercy upon me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for I _am_ weak: O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, heal me; for my bones are vexed.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>My soul is also sore vexed: but thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, how long?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Return, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, deliver my soul: oh save me for thy mercies’ sake.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For in death _there is_ no remembrance of thee: in the grave who shall give thee thanks?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I am weary with my groaning; all the night make I my bed to swim; I water my couch with my tears.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Mine eye is consumed because of grief; it waxeth old because of all mine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath heard the voice of my weeping.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath heard my supplication; the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will receive my prayer.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Let all mine enemies be ashamed and sore vexed: let them return _and_ be ashamed suddenly.  

## PSALM 7.

<div class="psalm-title">Shiggaion of David, which he sang unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, concerning the words of Cush the Benjamite.</div>

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, in thee do I put my trust: save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Lest he tear my soul like a lion, rending _it_ in pieces, while _there is_ none to deliver.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, if I have done this; if there be iniquity in my hands;  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>If I have rewarded evil unto him that was at peace with me; (yea, I have delivered him that without cause is mine enemy:)  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Let the enemy persecute my soul, and take _it_; yea, let him tread down my life upon the earth, and lay mine honour in the dust. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Arise, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, in thine anger, lift up thyself because of the rage of mine enemies: and awake for me _to_ the judgment _that_ thou hast commanded.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>So shall the congregation of the people compass thee about: for their sakes therefore return thou on high.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall judge the people: judge me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, according to my righteousness, and according to mine integrity _that is_ in me.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end; but establish the just: for the righteous God trieth the hearts and reins.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ My defence _is_ of God, which saveth the upright in heart.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>God judgeth the righteous, and God is angry _with the wicked_ every day.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>If he turn not, he will whet his sword; he hath bent his bow, and made it ready.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>He hath also prepared for him the instruments of death; he ordaineth his arrows against the persecutors.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, and hath conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>He made a pit, and digged it, and is fallen into the ditch _which_ he made.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>His mischief shall return upon his own head, and his violent dealing shall come down upon his own pate.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>I will praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> according to his righteousness: and will sing praise to the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> most high.  

## PSALM 8.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm of David.</div>

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our Lord, how excellent _is_ thy name in all the earth! who hast set thy glory above the heavens.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou ordained strength because of thine enemies, that thou mightest still the enemy and the avenger.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>¶ When I consider thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, the moon and the stars, which thou hast ordained;  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>What is man, that thou art mindful of him? and the son of man, that thou visitest him?  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For thou hast made him a little lower than the angels, and hast crowned him with glory and honour.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thou madest him to have dominion over the works of thy hands; thou hast put all _things_ under his feet:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>All sheep and oxen, yea, and the beasts of the field;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The fowl of the air, and the fish of the sea, _and whatsoever_ passeth through the paths of the seas.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our Lord, how excellent _is_ thy name in all the earth!  

## PSALM 9.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Muthlabben, A Psalm of David.</div>

I will praise _thee_, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, with my whole heart; I will shew forth all thy marvellous works.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will sing praise to thy name, O thou most High.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>When mine enemies are turned back, they shall fall and perish at thy presence.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For thou hast maintained my right and my cause; thou satest in the throne judging right.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou hast rebuked the heathen, thou hast destroyed the wicked, thou hast put out their name for ever and ever.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>O thou enemy, destructions are come to a perpetual end: and thou hast destroyed cities; their memorial is perished with them.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>But the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall endure for ever: he hath prepared his throne for judgment.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>And he shall judge the world in righteousness, he shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> also will be a refuge for the oppressed, a refuge in times of trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>And they that know thy name will put their trust in thee: for thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hast not forsaken them that seek thee.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ Sing praises to the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, which dwelleth in Zion: declare among the people his doings.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>When he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth them: he forgetteth not the cry of the humble.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Have mercy upon me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; consider my trouble _which I suffer_ of them that hate me, thou that liftest me up from the gates of death:  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>That I may shew forth all thy praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion: I will rejoice in thy salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>The heathen are sunk down in the pit _that_ they made: in the net which they hid is their own foot taken.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> is known _by_ the judgment _which_ he executeth: the wicked is snared in the work of his own hands. Higgaion. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The wicked shall be turned into hell, _and_ all the nations that forget God.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>For the needy shall not alway be forgotten: the expectation of the poor shall _not_ perish for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Arise, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; let not man prevail: let the heathen be judged in thy sight.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Put them in fear, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: _that_ the nations may know themselves _to be but_ men. Selah.  

## PSALM 10.

Why standest thou afar off, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? _why_ hidest thou _thyself_ in times of trouble?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The wicked in _his_ pride doth persecute the poor: let them be taken in the devices that they have imagined.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For the wicked boasteth of his heart’s desire, and blesseth the covetous, _whom_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> abhorreth.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, will not seek _after God_: God _is_ not in all his thoughts.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>His ways are always grievous; thy judgments _are_ far above out of his sight: _as for_ all his enemies, he puffeth at them.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He hath said in his heart, I shall not be moved: for _I shall_ never _be_ in adversity.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud: under his tongue _is_ mischief and vanity.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>He sitteth in the lurking places of the villages: in the secret places doth he murder the innocent: his eyes are privily set against the poor.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He lieth in wait secretly as a lion in his den: he lieth in wait to catch the poor: he doth catch the poor, when he draweth him into his net.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>He croucheth, _and_ humbleth himself, that the poor may fall by his strong ones.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>He hath said in his heart, God hath forgotten: he hideth his face; he will never see _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ Arise, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; O God, lift up thine hand: forget not the humble.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Wherefore doth the wicked contemn God? he hath said in his heart, Thou wilt not require _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Thou hast seen _it_; for thou beholdest mischief and spite, to requite _it_ with thy hand: the poor committeth himself unto thee; thou art the helper of the fatherless.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Break thou the arm of the wicked and the evil _man_: seek out his wickedness _till_ thou find none.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ King for ever and ever: the heathen are perished out of his land.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou hast heard the desire of the humble: thou wilt prepare their heart, thou wilt cause thine ear to hear:  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>To judge the fatherless and the oppressed, that the man of the earth may no more oppress.  

## PSALM 11.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, <em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

In the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> put I my trust: how say ye to my soul, Flee _as_ a bird to your mountain?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For, lo, the wicked bend _their_ bow, they make ready their arrow upon the string, that they may privily shoot at the upright in heart.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>If the foundations be destroyed, what can the righteous do?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ in his holy temple, the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span> throne _is_ in heaven: his eyes behold, his eyelids try, the children of men.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> trieth the righteous: but the wicked and him that loveth violence his soul hateth.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Upon the wicked he shall rain snares, fire and brimstone, and an horrible tempest: _this shall be_ the portion of their cup.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>For the righteous <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> loveth righteousness; his countenance doth behold the upright.  

## PSALM 12.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Sheminith, A Psalm of David.</div>

Help, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for the godly man ceaseth; for the faithful fail from among the children of men.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>They speak vanity every one with his neighbour: _with_ flattering lips _and_ with a double heart do they speak.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall cut off all flattering lips, _and_ the tongue that speaketh proud things:  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Who have said, With our tongue will we prevail; our lips _are_ our own: who _is_ lord over us?  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For the oppression of the poor, for the sighing of the needy, now will I arise, saith the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; I will set _him_ in safety _from him that_ puffeth at him.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The words of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _are_ pure words: _as_ silver tried in a furnace of earth, purified seven times.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Thou shalt keep them, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou shalt preserve them from this generation for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The wicked walk on every side, when the vilest men are exalted.  

## PSALM 13.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

How long wilt thou forget me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? for ever? how long wilt thou hide thy face from me?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>How long shall I take counsel in my soul, _having_ sorrow in my heart daily? how long shall mine enemy be exalted over me?  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Consider _and_ hear me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God: lighten mine eyes, lest I sleep the _sleep of_ death;  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Lest mine enemy say, I have prevailed against him; _and_ those that trouble me rejoice when I am moved.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>But I have trusted in thy mercy; my heart shall rejoice in thy salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I will sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, because he hath dealt bountifully with me.  

## PSALM 14.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, <em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

The fool hath said in his heart, _There is_ no God. They are corrupt, they have done abominable works, _there is_ none that doeth good.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> looked down from heaven upon the children of men, to see if there were any that did understand, _and_ seek God.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>They are all gone aside, they are _all_ together become filthy: _there is_ none that doeth good, no, not one.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ Have all the workers of iniquity no knowledge? who eat up my people _as_ they eat bread, and call not upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>There were they in great fear: for God _is_ in the generation of the righteous.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Ye have shamed the counsel of the poor, because the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ his refuge.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Oh that the salvation of Israel _were come_ out of Zion! when the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> bringeth back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, _and_ Israel shall be glad.  

## PSALM 15.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

<span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, who shall abide in thy tabernacle? who shall dwell in thy holy hill?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>He that walketh uprightly, and worketh righteousness, and speaketh the truth in his heart.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>_He that_ backbiteth not with his tongue, nor doeth evil to his neighbour, nor taketh up a reproach against his neighbour.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>In whose eyes a vile person is contemned; but he honoureth them that fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. _He that_ sweareth to _his own_ hurt, and changeth not.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>_He that_ putteth not out his money to usury, nor taketh reward against the innocent. He that doeth these _things_ shall never be moved.  

## PSALM 16.

<div class="psalm-title">Michtam of David.</div>

Preserve me, O God: for in thee do I put my trust.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>_O my soul_, thou hast said unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, Thou _art_ my Lord: my goodness _extendeth_ not to thee;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>_But_ to the saints that _are_ in the earth, and _to_ the excellent, in whom _is_ all my delight.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Their sorrows shall be multiplied _that_ hasten _after_ another _god_: their drink offerings of blood will I not offer, nor take up their names into my lips.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ the portion of mine inheritance and of my cup: thou maintainest my lot.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The lines are fallen unto me in pleasant _places_; yea, I have a goodly heritage.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>I will bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, who hath given me counsel: my reins also instruct me in the night seasons.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ I have set the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> always before me: because _he is_ at my right hand, I shall not be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Therefore my heart is glad, and my glory rejoiceth: my flesh also shall rest in hope.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For thou wilt not leave my soul in hell; neither wilt thou suffer thine Holy One to see corruption.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Thou wilt shew me the path of life: in thy presence _is_ fulness of joy; at thy right hand _there are_ pleasures for evermore.  

## PSALM 17.

<div class="psalm-title">A Prayer of David.</div>

Hear the right, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, attend unto my cry, give ear unto my prayer, _that goeth_ not out of feigned lips.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let my sentence come forth from thy presence; let thine eyes behold the things that are equal.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thou hast proved mine heart; thou hast visited _me_ in the night; thou hast tried me, _and_ shalt find nothing; I am purposed _that_ my mouth shall not transgress.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Concerning the works of men, by the word of thy lips I have kept _me from_ the paths of the destroyer.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Hold up my goings in thy paths, _that_ my footsteps slip not.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I have called upon thee, for thou wilt hear me, O God: incline thine ear unto me, _and hear_ my speech.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Shew thy marvellous lovingkindness, O thou that savest by thy right hand them which put their trust _in thee_ from those that rise up _against them_.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Keep me as the apple of the eye, hide me under the shadow of thy wings,  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>From the wicked that oppress me, _from_ my deadly enemies, _who_ compass me about.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>They are inclosed in their own fat: with their mouth they speak proudly.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>They have now compassed us in our steps: they have set their eyes bowing down to the earth;  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Like as a lion _that_ is greedy of his prey, and as it were a young lion lurking in secret places.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Arise, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, disappoint him, cast him down: deliver my soul from the wicked, _which is_ thy sword:  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>From men _which are_ thy hand, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, from men of the world, _which have_ their portion in _this_ life, and whose belly thou fillest with thy hid _treasure_: they are full of children, and leave the rest of their _substance_ to their babes.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>As for me, I will behold thy face in righteousness: I shall be satisfied, when I awake, with thy likeness.  

## PSALM 18.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, <em>A Psalm</em> of David, the servant of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, who spake unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> the words of this song in the day <em>that</em> the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> delivered him from the hand of all his enemies, and from the hand of Saul: And he said,</div>

I will love thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, my strength.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ my rock, and my fortress, and my deliverer; my God, my strength, in whom I will trust; my buckler, and the horn of my salvation, _and_ my high tower.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>I will call upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _who is worthy_ to be praised: so shall I be saved from mine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The sorrows of death compassed me, and the floods of ungodly men made me afraid.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The sorrows of hell compassed me about: the snares of death prevented me.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>In my distress I called upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and cried unto my God: he heard my voice out of his temple, and my cry came before him, _even_ into his ears.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Then the earth shook and trembled; the foundations also of the hills moved and were shaken, because he was wroth.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>There went up a smoke out of his nostrils, and fire out of his mouth devoured: coals were kindled by it.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He bowed the heavens also, and came down: and darkness _was_ under his feet.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>And he rode upon a cherub, and did fly: yea, he did fly upon the wings of the wind.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>He made darkness his secret place; his pavilion round about him _were_ dark waters _and_ thick clouds of the skies.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>At the brightness _that was_ before him his thick clouds passed, hail _stones_ and coals of fire.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> also thundered in the heavens, and the Highest gave his voice; hail _stones_ and coals of fire.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Yea, he sent out his arrows, and scattered them; and he shot out lightnings, and discomfited them.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Then the channels of waters were seen, and the foundations of the world were discovered at thy rebuke, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, at the blast of the breath of thy nostrils.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>He sent from above, he took me, he drew me out of many waters.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>He delivered me from my strong enemy, and from them which hated me: for they were too strong for me.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>They prevented me in the day of my calamity: but the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> was my stay.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>He brought me forth also into a large place; he delivered me, because he delighted in me.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>¶ The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> rewarded me according to my righteousness; according to the cleanness of my hands hath he recompensed me.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>For I have kept the ways of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and have not wickedly departed from my God.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>For all his judgments _were_ before me, and I did not put away his statutes from me.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>I was also upright before him, and I kept myself from mine iniquity.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Therefore hath the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> recompensed me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in his eyesight.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>With the merciful thou wilt shew thyself merciful; with an upright man thou wilt shew thyself upright;  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>With the pure thou wilt shew thyself pure; and with the froward thou wilt shew thyself froward.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>For thou wilt save the afflicted people; but wilt bring down high looks.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>For thou wilt light my candle: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God will enlighten my darkness.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>¶ For by thee I have run through a troop; and by my God have I leaped over a wall.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>_As for_ God, his way _is_ perfect: the word of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> is tried: he _is_ a buckler to all those that trust in him.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>For who _is_ God save the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? or who _is_ a rock save our God?  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>_It is_ God that girdeth me with strength, and maketh my way perfect.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>He maketh my feet like hinds’ _feet_, and setteth me upon my high places.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>He teacheth my hands to war, so that a bow of steel is broken by mine arms.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>Thou hast also given me the shield of thy salvation: and thy right hand hath holden me up, and thy gentleness hath made me great.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>Thou hast enlarged my steps under me, that my feet did not slip.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>I have pursued mine enemies, and overtaken them: neither did I turn again till they were consumed.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>I have wounded them that they were not able to rise: they are fallen under my feet.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>For thou hast girded me with strength unto the battle: thou hast subdued under me those that rose up against me.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>Thou hast also given me the necks of mine enemies; that I might destroy them that hate me.  
<span class="verse-number">41&ensp;</span>They cried, but _there was_ none to save _them: even_ unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, but he answered them not.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>Then did I beat them small as the dust before the wind: I did cast them out as the dirt in the streets.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>Thou hast delivered me from the strivings of the people; _and_ thou hast made me the head of the heathen: a people _whom_ I have not known shall serve me.  
<span class="verse-number">44&ensp;</span>As soon as they hear of me, they shall obey me: the strangers shall submit themselves unto me.  
<span class="verse-number">45&ensp;</span>The strangers shall fade away, and be afraid out of their close places.  
<span class="verse-number">46&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> liveth; and blessed _be_ my rock; and let the God of my salvation be exalted.  
<span class="verse-number">47&ensp;</span>_It is_ God that avengeth me, and subdueth the people under me.  
<span class="verse-number">48&ensp;</span>He delivereth me from mine enemies: yea, thou liftest me up above those that rise up against me: thou hast delivered me from the violent man.  
<span class="verse-number">49&ensp;</span>Therefore will I give thanks unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, among the heathen, and sing praises unto thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">50&ensp;</span>Great deliverance giveth he to his king; and sheweth mercy to his anointed, to David, and to his seed for evermore.  

## PSALM 19.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

The heavens declare the glory of God; and the firmament sheweth his handywork.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Day unto day uttereth speech, and night unto night sheweth knowledge.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>_There is_ no speech nor language, _where_ their voice is not heard.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Their line is gone out through all the earth, and their words to the end of the world. In them hath he set a tabernacle for the sun,  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Which _is_ as a bridegroom coming out of his chamber, _and_ rejoiceth as a strong man to run a race.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>His going forth _is_ from the end of the heaven, and his circuit unto the ends of it: and there is nothing hid from the heat thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ The law of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ perfect, converting the soul: the testimony of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ sure, making wise the simple.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The statutes of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _are_ right, rejoicing the heart: the commandment of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ pure, enlightening the eyes.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The fear of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ clean, enduring for ever: the judgments of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _are_ true _and_ righteous altogether.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>More to be desired _are they_ than gold, yea, than much fine gold: sweeter also than honey and the honeycomb.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Moreover by them is thy servant warned: _and_ in keeping of them _there is_ great reward.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Who can understand _his_ errors? cleanse thou me from secret _faults_.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Keep back thy servant also from presumptuous _sins_; let them not have dominion over me: then shall I be upright, and I shall be innocent from the great transgression.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart, be acceptable in thy sight, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, my strength, and my redeemer.  

## PSALM 20.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hear thee in the day of trouble; the name of the God of Jacob defend thee;  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Send thee help from the sanctuary, and strengthen thee out of Zion;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Remember all thy offerings, and accept thy burnt sacrifice; Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Grant thee according to thine own heart, and fulfil all thy counsel.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>We will rejoice in thy salvation, and in the name of our God we will set up _our_ banners: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> fulfil all thy petitions.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Now know I that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> saveth his anointed; he will hear him from his holy heaven with the saving strength of his right hand.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Some _trust_ in chariots, and some in horses: but we will remember the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They are brought down and fallen: but we are risen, and stand upright.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Save, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: let the king hear us when we call.  

## PSALM 21.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

The king shall joy in thy strength, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and in thy salvation how greatly shall he rejoice!  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thou hast given him his heart’s desire, and hast not withholden the request of his lips. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For thou preventest him with the blessings of goodness: thou settest a crown of pure gold on his head.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He asked life of thee, _and_ thou gavest _it_ him, _even_ length of days for ever and ever.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>His glory _is_ great in thy salvation: honour and majesty hast thou laid upon him.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>For thou hast made him most blessed for ever: thou hast made him exceeding glad with thy countenance.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ For the king trusteth in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and through the mercy of the most High he shall not be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Thine hand shall find out all thine enemies: thy right hand shall find out those that hate thee.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou shalt make them as a fiery oven in the time of thine anger: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall swallow them up in his wrath, and the fire shall devour them.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Their fruit shalt thou destroy from the earth, and their seed from among the children of men.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>For they intended evil against thee: they imagined a mischievous device, _which_ they are not able _to perform_.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Therefore shalt thou make them turn their back, _when_ thou shalt make ready _thine arrows_ upon thy strings against the face of them.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Be thou exalted, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, in thine own strength: _so_ will we sing and praise thy power.  

## PSALM 22.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Aijeleth Shahar, A Psalm of David.</div>

My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me? _why art thou so_ far from helping me, _and from_ the words of my roaring?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>O my God, I cry in the daytime, but thou hearest not; and in the night season, and am not silent.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>But thou _art_ holy, _O thou_ that inhabitest the praises of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Our fathers trusted in thee: they trusted, and thou didst deliver them.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They cried unto thee, and were delivered: they trusted in thee, and were not confounded.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>But I _am_ a worm, and no man; a reproach of men, and despised of the people.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>All they that see me laugh me to scorn: they shoot out the lip, they shake the head, _saying_,  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>He trusted on the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _that_ he would deliver him: let him deliver him, seeing he delighted in him.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>But thou _art_ he that took me out of the womb: thou didst make me hope _when I was_ upon my mother’s breasts.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>I was cast upon thee from the womb: thou _art_ my God from my mother’s belly.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ Be not far from me; for trouble _is_ near; for _there is_ none to help.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Many bulls have compassed me: strong _bulls_ of Bashan have beset me round.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>They gaped upon me _with_ their mouths, _as_ a ravening and a roaring lion.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>I am poured out like water, and all my bones are out of joint: my heart is like wax; it is melted in the midst of my bowels.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>My strength is dried up like a potsherd; and my tongue cleaveth to my jaws; and thou hast brought me into the dust of death.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>For dogs have compassed me: the assembly of the wicked have inclosed me: they pierced my hands and my feet.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>I may tell all my bones: they look _and_ stare upon me.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>They part my garments among them, and cast lots upon my vesture.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>But be not thou far from me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: O my strength, haste thee to help me.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Deliver my soul from the sword; my darling from the power of the dog.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Save me from the lion’s mouth: for thou hast heard me from the horns of the unicorns.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>¶ I will declare thy name unto my brethren: in the midst of the congregation will I praise thee.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Ye that fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, praise him; all ye the seed of Jacob, glorify him; and fear him, all ye the seed of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>For he hath not despised nor abhorred the affliction of the afflicted; neither hath he hid his face from him; but when he cried unto him, he heard.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>My praise _shall be_ of thee in the great congregation: I will pay my vows before them that fear him.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>The meek shall eat and be satisfied: they shall praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> that seek him: your heart shall live for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>All the ends of the world shall remember and turn unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: and all the kindreds of the nations shall worship before thee.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>For the kingdom _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span>: and he _is_ the governor among the nations.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>All _they that be_ fat upon earth shall eat and worship: all they that go down to the dust shall bow before him: and none can keep alive his own soul.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>A seed shall serve him; it shall be accounted to the Lord for a generation.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>They shall come, and shall declare his righteousness unto a people that shall be born, that he hath done _this_.  

## PSALM 23.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ my shepherd; I shall not want.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>He maketh me to lie down in green pastures: he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>He restoreth my soul: he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name’s sake.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil: for thou _art_ with me; thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies: thou anointest my head with oil; my cup runneth over.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life: and I will dwell in the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> for ever.  

## PSALM 24.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

The earth _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span>, and the fulness thereof; the world, and they that dwell therein.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For he hath founded it upon the seas, and established it upon the floods.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>¶ Who shall ascend into the hill of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? or who shall stand in his holy place?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He that hath clean hands, and a pure heart; who hath not lifted up his soul unto vanity, nor sworn deceitfully.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>He shall receive the blessing from the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and righteousness from the God of his salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>This _is_ the generation of them that seek him, that seek thy face, O Jacob. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Lift up your heads, O ye gates; and be ye lift up, ye everlasting doors; and the King of glory shall come in.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Who _is_ this King of glory? The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> strong and mighty, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> mighty in battle.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Lift up your heads, O ye gates; even lift _them_ up, ye everlasting doors; and the King of glory shall come in.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Who is this King of glory? The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts, he _is_ the King of glory. Selah.  

## PSALM 25.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, do I lift up my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>O my God, I trust in thee: let me not be ashamed, let not mine enemies triumph over me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Yea, let none that wait on thee be ashamed: let them be ashamed which transgress without cause.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Shew me thy ways, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; teach me thy paths.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Lead me in thy truth, and teach me: for thou _art_ the God of my salvation; on thee do I wait all the day.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Remember, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thy tender mercies and thy lovingkindnesses; for they _have been_ ever of old.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions: according to thy mercy remember thou me for thy goodness’ sake, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Good and upright _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: therefore will he teach sinners in the way.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The meek will he guide in judgment: and the meek will he teach his way.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>All the paths of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _are_ mercy and truth unto such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>For thy name’s sake, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, pardon mine iniquity; for it _is_ great.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>What man _is_ he that feareth the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? him shall he teach in the way _that_ he shall choose.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>His soul shall dwell at ease; and his seed shall inherit the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>The secret of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ with them that fear him; and he will shew them his covenant.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>¶ Mine eyes _are_ ever toward the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for he shall pluck my feet out of the net.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Turn thee unto me, and have mercy upon me; for I _am_ desolate and afflicted.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The troubles of my heart are enlarged: _O_ bring thou me out of my distresses.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Look upon mine affliction and my pain; and forgive all my sins.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Consider mine enemies; for they are many; and they hate me with cruel hatred.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>O keep my soul, and deliver me: let me not be ashamed; for I put my trust in thee.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Let integrity and uprightness preserve me; for I wait on thee.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Redeem Israel, O God, out of all his troubles.  

## PSALM 26.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Judge me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for I have walked in mine integrity: I have trusted also in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; _therefore_ I shall not slide.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Examine me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and prove me; try my reins and my heart.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For thy lovingkindness _is_ before mine eyes: and I have walked in thy truth.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I have not sat with vain persons, neither will I go in with dissemblers.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I have hated the congregation of evil doers; and will not sit with the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ I will wash mine hands in innocency: so will I compass thine altar, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>That I may publish with the voice of thanksgiving, and tell of all thy wondrous works.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, I have loved the habitation of thy house, and the place where thine honour dwelleth.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Gather not my soul with sinners, nor my life with bloody men:  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>In whose hands _is_ mischief, and their right hand is full of bribes.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>But as for me, I will walk in mine integrity: redeem me, and be merciful unto me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>My foot standeth in an even place: in the congregations will I bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 27.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ my light and my salvation; whom shall I fear? the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ the strength of my life; of whom shall I be afraid?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>When the wicked, _even_ mine enemies and my foes, came upon me to eat up my flesh, they stumbled and fell.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Though an host should encamp against me, my heart shall not fear: though war should rise against me, in this _will_ I _be_ confident.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>One _thing_ have I desired of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, that will I seek after; that I may dwell in the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> all the days of my life, to behold the beauty of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and to enquire in his temple.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For in the time of trouble he shall hide me in his pavilion: in the secret of his tabernacle shall he hide me; he shall set me up upon a rock.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>And now shall mine head be lifted up above mine enemies round about me: therefore will I offer in his tabernacle sacrifices of joy; I will sing, yea, I will sing praises unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Hear, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _when_ I cry with my voice: have mercy also upon me, and answer me.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>_When thou saidst_, Seek ye my face; my heart said unto thee, Thy face, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, will I seek.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Hide not thy face _far_ from me; put not thy servant away in anger: thou hast been my help; leave me not, neither forsake me, O God of my salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>When my father and my mother forsake me, then the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will take me up.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Teach me thy way, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and lead me in a plain path, because of mine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Deliver me not over unto the will of mine enemies: for false witnesses are risen up against me, and such as breathe out cruelty.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>_I had fainted_, unless I had believed to see the goodness of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in the land of the living.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Wait on the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: be of good courage, and he shall strengthen thine heart: wait, I say, on the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 28.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Unto thee will I cry, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my rock; be not silent to me: lest, _if_ thou be silent to me, I become like them that go down into the pit.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Hear the voice of my supplications, when I cry unto thee, when I lift up my hands toward thy holy oracle.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Draw me not away with the wicked, and with the workers of iniquity, which speak peace to their neighbours, but mischief _is_ in their hearts.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Give them according to their deeds, and according to the wickedness of their endeavours: give them after the work of their hands; render to them their desert.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Because they regard not the works of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, nor the operation of his hands, he shall destroy them, and not build them up.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, because he hath heard the voice of my supplications.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ my strength and my shield; my heart trusted in him, and I am helped: therefore my heart greatly rejoiceth; and with my song will I praise him.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ their strength, and he _is_ the saving strength of his anointed.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Save thy people, and bless thine inheritance: feed them also, and lift them up for ever.  

## PSALM 29.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

Give unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O ye mighty, give unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> glory and strength.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Give unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> the glory due unto his name; worship the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in the beauty of holiness.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ upon the waters: the God of glory thundereth: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ upon many waters.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ powerful; the voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ full of majesty.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> breaketh the cedars; yea, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> breaketh the cedars of Lebanon.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He maketh them also to skip like a calf; Lebanon and Sirion like a young unicorn.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> divideth the flames of fire.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shaketh the wilderness; the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shaketh the wilderness of Kadesh.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> maketh the hinds to calve, and discovereth the forests: and in his temple doth every one speak of _his_ glory.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> sitteth upon the flood; yea, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> sitteth King for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will give strength unto his people; the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will bless his people with peace.  

## PSALM 30.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm <em>and</em> Song <em>at</em> the dedication of the house of David.</div>

I will extol thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for thou hast lifted me up, and hast not made my foes to rejoice over me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, I cried unto thee, and thou hast healed me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou hast brought up my soul from the grave: thou hast kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O ye saints of his, and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For his anger _endureth but_ a moment; in his favour _is_ life: weeping may endure for a night, but joy _cometh_ in the morning.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ And in my prosperity I said, I shall never be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, by thy favour thou hast made my mountain to stand strong: thou didst hide thy face, _and_ I was troubled.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I cried to thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> I made supplication.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>What profit _is there_ in my blood, when I go down to the pit? Shall the dust praise thee? shall it declare thy truth?  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Hear, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and have mercy upon me: <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, be thou my helper.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Thou hast turned for me my mourning into dancing: thou hast put off my sackcloth, and girded me with gladness;  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>To the end that _my_ glory may sing praise to thee, and not be silent. O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, I will give thanks unto thee for ever.  

## PSALM 31.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

In thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, do I put my trust; let me never be ashamed: deliver me in thy righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Bow down thine ear to me; deliver me speedily: be thou my strong rock, for an house of defence to save me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For thou _art_ my rock and my fortress; therefore for thy name’s sake lead me, and guide me.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Pull me out of the net that they have laid privily for me: for thou _art_ my strength.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Into thine hand I commit my spirit: thou hast redeemed me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of truth.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I have hated them that regard lying vanities: but I trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>I will be glad and rejoice in thy mercy: for thou hast considered my trouble; thou hast known my soul in adversities;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>And hast not shut me up into the hand of the enemy: thou hast set my feet in a large room.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ Have mercy upon me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, for I am in trouble: mine eye is consumed with grief, _yea_, my soul and my belly.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For my life is spent with grief, and my years with sighing: my strength faileth because of mine iniquity, and my bones are consumed.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>I was a reproach among all mine enemies, but especially among my neighbours, and a fear to mine acquaintance: they that did see me without fled from me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>I am forgotten as a dead man out of mind: I am like a broken vessel.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>For I have heard the slander of many: fear _was_ on every side: while they took counsel together against me, they devised to take away my life.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>But I trusted in thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: I said, Thou _art_ my God.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>My times _are_ in thy hand: deliver me from the hand of mine enemies, and from them that persecute me.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: save me for thy mercies’ sake.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Let me not be ashamed, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for I have called upon thee: let the wicked be ashamed, _and_ let them be silent in the grave.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Let the lying lips be put to silence; which speak grievous things proudly and contemptuously against the righteous.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>¶ _Oh_ how great _is_ thy goodness, which thou hast laid up for them that fear thee; _which_ thou hast wrought for them that trust in thee before the sons of men!  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Thou shalt hide them in the secret of thy presence from the pride of man: thou shalt keep them secretly in a pavilion from the strife of tongues.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for he hath shewed me his marvellous kindness in a strong city.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>For I said in my haste, I am cut off from before thine eyes: nevertheless thou heardest the voice of my supplications when I cried unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>O love the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all ye his saints: _for_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> preserveth the faithful, and plentifully rewardeth the proud doer.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Be of good courage, and he shall strengthen your heart, all ye that hope in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 32.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David, Maschil.</div>

Blessed _is he whose_ transgression _is_ forgiven, _whose_ sin _is_ covered.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Blessed _is_ the man unto whom the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> imputeth not iniquity, and in whose spirit _there is_ no guile.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>When I kept silence, my bones waxed old through my roaring all the day long.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For day and night thy hand was heavy upon me: my moisture is turned into the drought of summer. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I acknowledged my sin unto thee, and mine iniquity have I not hid. I said, I will confess my transgressions unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and thou forgavest the iniquity of my sin. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>For this shall every one that is godly pray unto thee in a time when thou mayest be found: surely in the floods of great waters they shall not come nigh unto him.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Thou _art_ my hiding place; thou shalt preserve me from trouble; thou shalt compass me about with songs of deliverance. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I will instruct thee and teach thee in the way which thou shalt go: I will guide thee with mine eye.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Be ye not as the horse, _or_ as the mule, _which_ have no understanding: whose mouth must be held in with bit and bridle, lest they come near unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Many sorrows _shall be_ to the wicked: but he that trusteth in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, mercy shall compass him about.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Be glad in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and rejoice, ye righteous: and shout for joy, all _ye that are_ upright in heart.  

## PSALM 33.

Rejoice in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O ye righteous: _for_ praise is comely for the upright.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with harp: sing unto him with the psaltery _and_ an instrument of ten strings.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Sing unto him a new song; play skilfully with a loud noise.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For the word of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ right; and all his works _are done_ in truth.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>He loveth righteousness and judgment: the earth is full of the goodness of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>By the word of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> were the heavens made; and all the host of them by the breath of his mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He gathereth the waters of the sea together as an heap: he layeth up the depth in storehouses.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Let all the earth fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For he spake, and it was _done_; he commanded, and it stood fast.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> bringeth the counsel of the heathen to nought: he maketh the devices of the people of none effect.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The counsel of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> standeth for ever, the thoughts of his heart to all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ Blessed _is_ the nation whose God _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; _and_ the people _whom_ he hath chosen for his own inheritance.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> looketh from heaven; he beholdeth all the sons of men.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>From the place of his habitation he looketh upon all the inhabitants of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>He fashioneth their hearts alike; he considereth all their works.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>There is no king saved by the multitude of an host: a mighty man is not delivered by much strength.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>An horse _is_ a vain thing for safety: neither shall he deliver _any_ by his great strength.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Behold, the eye of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ upon them that fear him, upon them that hope in his mercy;  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>To deliver their soul from death, and to keep them alive in famine.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Our soul waiteth for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: he _is_ our help and our shield.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>For our heart shall rejoice in him, because we have trusted in his holy name.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Let thy mercy, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, be upon us, according as we hope in thee.  

## PSALM 34.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David, when he changed his behaviour before Abimelech; who drove him away, and he departed.</div>

I will bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> at all times: his praise _shall_ continually _be_ in my mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>My soul shall make her boast in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: the humble shall hear _thereof_, and be glad.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>O magnify the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with me, and let us exalt his name together.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I sought the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and he heard me, and delivered me from all my fears.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They looked unto him, and were lightened: and their faces were not ashamed.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>This poor man cried, and the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> heard _him_, and saved him out of all his troubles.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The angel of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> encampeth round about them that fear him, and delivereth them.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>O taste and see that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ good: blessed _is_ the man _that_ trusteth in him.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>O fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, ye his saints: for _there is_ no want to them that fear him.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger: but they that seek the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall not want any good _thing_.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ Come, ye children, hearken unto me: I will teach you the fear of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>What man _is he that_ desireth life, _and_ loveth _many_ days, that he may see good?  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Keep thy tongue from evil, and thy lips from speaking guile.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Depart from evil, and do good; seek peace, and pursue it.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>The eyes of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _are_ upon the righteous, and his ears _are open_ unto their cry.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The face of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ against them that do evil, to cut off the remembrance of them from the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>_The righteous_ cry, and the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> heareth, and delivereth them out of all their troubles.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ nigh unto them that are of a broken heart; and saveth such as be of a contrite spirit.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Many _are_ the afflictions of the righteous: but the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> delivereth him out of them all.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>He keepeth all his bones: not one of them is broken.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Evil shall slay the wicked: and they that hate the righteous shall be desolate.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> redeemeth the soul of his servants: and none of them that trust in him shall be desolate.  

## PSALM 35.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Plead _my cause_, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, with them that strive with me: fight against them that fight against me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Take hold of shield and buckler, and stand up for mine help.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Draw out also the spear, and stop _the way_ against them that persecute me: say unto my soul, I _am_ thy salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Let them be confounded and put to shame that seek after my soul: let them be turned back and brought to confusion that devise my hurt.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Let them be as chaff before the wind: and let the angel of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> chase _them_.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Let their way be dark and slippery: and let the angel of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> persecute them.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>For without cause have they hid for me their net _in_ a pit, _which_ without cause they have digged for my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Let destruction come upon him at unawares; and let his net that he hath hid catch himself: into that very destruction let him fall.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>And my soul shall be joyful in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: it shall rejoice in his salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>All my bones shall say, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, who _is_ like unto thee, which deliverest the poor from him that is too strong for him, yea, the poor and the needy from him that spoileth him?  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ False witnesses did rise up; they laid to my charge _things_ that I knew not.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>They rewarded me evil for good _to_ the spoiling of my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing _was_ sackcloth: I humbled my soul with fasting; and my prayer returned into mine own bosom.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>I behaved myself as though _he had been_ my friend _or_ brother: I bowed down heavily, as one that mourneth _for his_ mother.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>But in mine adversity they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together: _yea_, the abjects gathered themselves together against me, and I knew _it_ not; they did tear _me_, and ceased not:  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>With hypocritical mockers in feasts, they gnashed upon me with their teeth.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>¶ Lord, how long wilt thou look on? rescue my soul from their destructions, my darling from the lions.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>I will give thee thanks in the great congregation: I will praise thee among much people.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Let not them that are mine enemies wrongfully rejoice over me: _neither_ let them wink with the eye that hate me without a cause.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>For they speak not peace: but they devise deceitful matters against _them that are_ quiet in the land.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Yea, they opened their mouth wide against me, _and_ said, Aha, aha, our eye hath seen _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>_This_ thou hast seen, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: keep not silence: O Lord, be not far from me.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Stir up thyself, and awake to my judgment, _even_ unto my cause, my God and my Lord.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Judge me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, according to thy righteousness; and let them not rejoice over me.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Let them not say in their hearts, Ah, so would we have it: let them not say, We have swallowed him up.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that rejoice at mine hurt: let them be clothed with shame and dishonour that magnify _themselves_ against me.
