<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>Let them shout for joy, and be glad, that favour my righteous cause: yea, let them say continually, Let the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> be magnified, which hath pleasure in the prosperity of his servant.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>And my tongue shall speak of thy righteousness _and_ of thy praise all the day long.  

## PSALM 36.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, <em>A Psalm</em> of David the servant of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.</div>

The transgression of the wicked saith within my heart, _that there is_ no fear of God before his eyes.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For he flattereth himself in his own eyes, until his iniquity be found to be hateful.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The words of his mouth _are_ iniquity and deceit: he hath left off to be wise, _and_ to do good.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He deviseth mischief upon his bed; he setteth himself in a way _that is_ not good; he abhorreth not evil.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ Thy mercy, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _is_ in the heavens; _and_ thy faithfulness _reacheth_ unto the clouds.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thy righteousness _is_ like the great mountains; thy judgments _are_ a great deep: O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou preservest man and beast.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>How excellent _is_ thy lovingkindness, O God! therefore the children of men put their trust under the shadow of thy wings.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of thy house; and thou shalt make them drink of the river of thy pleasures.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For with thee _is_ the fountain of life: in thy light shall we see light.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>O continue thy lovingkindness unto them that know thee; and thy righteousness to the upright in heart.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Let not the foot of pride come against me, and let not the hand of the wicked remove me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>There are the workers of iniquity fallen: they are cast down, and shall not be able to rise.  

## PSALM 37.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Fret not thyself because of evildoers, neither be thou envious against the workers of iniquity.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For they shall soon be cut down like the grass, and wither as the green herb.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and do good; _so_ shalt thou dwell in the land, and verily thou shalt be fed.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Delight thyself also in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and he shall give thee the desires of thine heart.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Commit thy way unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; trust also in him; and he shall bring _it_ to pass.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>And he shall bring forth thy righteousness as the light, and thy judgment as the noonday.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Rest in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and wait patiently for him: fret not thyself because of him who prospereth in his way, because of the man who bringeth wicked devices to pass.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Cease from anger, and forsake wrath: fret not thyself in any wise to do evil.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For evildoers shall be cut off: but those that wait upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, they shall inherit the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For yet a little while, and the wicked _shall_ not _be_: yea, thou shalt diligently consider his place, and it _shall_ not _be_.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>But the meek shall inherit the earth; and shall delight themselves in the abundance of peace.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>The wicked plotteth against the just, and gnasheth upon him with his teeth.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>The Lord shall laugh at him: for he seeth that his day is coming.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their bow, to cast down the poor and needy, _and_ to slay such as be of upright conversation.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Their sword shall enter into their own heart, and their bows shall be broken.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>A little that a righteous man hath _is_ better than the riches of many wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>For the arms of the wicked shall be broken: but the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> upholdeth the righteous.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> knoweth the days of the upright: and their inheritance shall be for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>They shall not be ashamed in the evil time: and in the days of famine they shall be satisfied.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>But the wicked shall perish, and the enemies of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _shall be_ as the fat of lambs: they shall consume; into smoke shall they consume away.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>¶ The wicked borroweth, and payeth not again: but the righteous sheweth mercy, and giveth.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>For _such as be_ blessed of him shall inherit the earth; and _they that be_ cursed of him shall be cut off.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>The steps of a _good_ man are ordered by the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: and he delighteth in his way.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Though he fall, he shall not be utterly cast down: for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> upholdeth _him with_ his hand.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>I have been young, and _now_ am old; yet have I not seen the righteous forsaken, nor his seed begging bread.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>_He is_ ever merciful, and lendeth; and his seed _is_ blessed.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>Depart from evil, and do good; and dwell for evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> loveth judgment, and forsaketh not his saints; they are preserved for ever: but the seed of the wicked shall be cut off.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>The righteous shall inherit the land, and dwell therein for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>The mouth of the righteous speaketh wisdom, and his tongue talketh of judgment.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>The law of his God _is_ in his heart; none of his steps shall slide.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>The wicked watcheth the righteous, and seeketh to slay him.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will not leave him in his hand, nor condemn him when he is judged.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>¶ Wait on the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and keep his way, and he shall exalt thee to inherit the land: when the wicked are cut off, thou shalt see _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>I have seen the wicked in great power, and spreading himself like a green bay tree.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>Yet he passed away, and, lo, he _was_ not: yea, I sought him, but he could not be found.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>Mark the perfect _man_, and behold the upright: for the end of _that_ man _is_ peace.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>But the transgressors shall be destroyed together: the end of the wicked shall be cut off.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>But the salvation of the righteous _is_ of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: _he is_ their strength in the time of trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>And the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall help them, and deliver them: he shall deliver them from the wicked, and save them, because they trust in him.  

## PSALM 38.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David, to bring to remembrance.</div>

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, rebuke me not in thy wrath: neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For thine arrows stick fast in me, and thy hand presseth me sore.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>_There is_ no soundness in my flesh because of thine anger; neither _is there any_ rest in my bones because of my sin.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For mine iniquities are gone over mine head: as an heavy burden they are too heavy for me.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>My wounds stink _and_ are corrupt because of my foolishness.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I am troubled; I am bowed down greatly; I go mourning all the day long.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>For my loins are filled with a loathsome _disease_: and _there is_ no soundness in my flesh.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I am feeble and sore broken: I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Lord, all my desire _is_ before thee; and my groaning is not hid from thee.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>My heart panteth, my strength faileth me: as for the light of mine eyes, it also is gone from me.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my sore; and my kinsmen stand afar off.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ They also that seek after my life lay snares _for me_: and they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and imagine deceits all the day long.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>But I, as a deaf _man_, heard not; and _I was_ as a dumb man _that_ openeth not his mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Thus I was as a man that heareth not, and in whose mouth _are_ no reproofs.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>For in thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, do I hope: thou wilt hear, O Lord my God.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>For I said, _Hear me_, lest _otherwise_ they should rejoice over me: when my foot slippeth, they magnify _themselves_ against me.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>For I _am_ ready to halt, and my sorrow _is_ continually before me.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>For I will declare mine iniquity; I will be sorry for my sin.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>But mine enemies _are_ lively, _and_ they are strong: and they that hate me wrongfully are multiplied.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>They also that render evil for good are mine adversaries; because I follow _the thing that_ good _is_.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Forsake me not, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: O my God, be not far from me.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Make haste to help me, O Lord my salvation.  

## PSALM 39.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, <em>even</em> to Jeduthun, A Psalm of David.</div>

I said, I will take heed to my ways, that I sin not with my tongue: I will keep my mouth with a bridle, while the wicked is before me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I was dumb with silence, I held my peace, _even_ from good; and my sorrow was stirred.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>My heart was hot within me, while I was musing the fire burned: _then_ spake I with my tongue,  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, make me to know mine end, and the measure of my days, what it _is; that_ I may know how frail I _am_.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Behold, thou hast made my days _as_ an handbreadth; and mine age _is_ as nothing before thee: verily every man at his best state _is_ altogether vanity. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Surely every man walketh in a vain shew: surely they are disquieted in vain: he heapeth up _riches_, and knoweth not who shall gather them.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ And now, Lord, what wait I for? my hope _is_ in thee.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Deliver me from all my transgressions: make me not the reproach of the foolish.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I was dumb, I opened not my mouth; because thou didst _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Remove thy stroke away from me: I am consumed by the blow of thine hand.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>When thou with rebukes dost correct man for iniquity, thou makest his beauty to consume away like a moth: surely every man _is_ vanity. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Hear my prayer, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and give ear unto my cry; hold not thy peace at my tears: for I _am_ a stranger with thee, _and_ a sojourner, as all my fathers _were_.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>O spare me, that I may recover strength, before I go hence, and be no more.  

## PSALM 40.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

I waited patiently for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and he inclined unto me, and heard my cry.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>He brought me up also out of an horrible pit, out of the miry clay, and set my feet upon a rock, _and_ established my goings.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>And he hath put a new song in my mouth, _even_ praise unto our God: many shall see _it_, and fear, and shall trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Blessed _is_ that man that maketh the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> his trust, and respecteth not the proud, nor such as turn aside to lies.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Many, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, _are_ thy wonderful works _which_ thou hast done, and thy thoughts _which are_ to us-ward: they cannot be reckoned up in order unto thee: _if_ I would declare and speak _of them_, they are more than can be numbered.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Sacrifice and offering thou didst not desire; mine ears hast thou opened: burnt offering and sin offering hast thou not required.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Then said I, Lo, I come: in the volume of the book _it is_ written of me,  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I delight to do thy will, O my God: yea, thy law _is_ within my heart.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I have preached righteousness in the great congregation: lo, I have not refrained my lips, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou knowest.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>I have not hid thy righteousness within my heart; I have declared thy faithfulness and thy salvation: I have not concealed thy lovingkindness and thy truth from the great congregation.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ Withhold not thou thy tender mercies from me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: let thy lovingkindness and thy truth continually preserve me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>For innumerable evils have compassed me about: mine iniquities have taken hold upon me, so that I am not able to look up; they are more than the hairs of mine head: therefore my heart faileth me.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Be pleased, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, to deliver me: O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, make haste to help me.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Let them be ashamed and confounded together that seek after my soul to destroy it; let them be driven backward and put to shame that wish me evil.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Let them be desolate for a reward of their shame that say unto me, Aha, aha.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: let such as love thy salvation say continually, The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> be magnified.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>But I _am_ poor and needy; _yet_ the Lord thinketh upon me: thou _art_ my help and my deliverer; make no tarrying, O my God.  

## PSALM 41.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

Blessed _is_ he that considereth the poor: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will deliver him in time of trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will preserve him, and keep him alive; _and_ he shall be blessed upon the earth: and thou wilt not deliver him unto the will of his enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will strengthen him upon the bed of languishing: thou wilt make all his bed in his sickness.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I said, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, be merciful unto me: heal my soul; for I have sinned against thee.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ Mine enemies speak evil of me, When shall he die, and his name perish?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>And if he come to see _me_, he speaketh vanity: his heart gathereth iniquity to itself; _when_ he goeth abroad, he telleth _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>All that hate me whisper together against me: against me do they devise my hurt.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>An evil disease, _say they_, cleaveth fast unto him: and _now_ that he lieth he shall rise up no more.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Yea, mine own familiar friend, in whom I trusted, which did eat of my bread, hath lifted up _his_ heel against me.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>But thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, be merciful unto me, and raise me up, that I may requite them.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>By this I know that thou favourest me, because mine enemy doth not triumph over me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>And as for me, thou upholdest me in mine integrity, and settest me before thy face for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of Israel from everlasting, and to everlasting. Amen, and Amen.  

### BOOK II.

## PSALM 42.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, Maschil, for the sons of Korah.</div>

As the hart panteth after the water brooks, so panteth my soul after thee, O God.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>My soul thirsteth for God, for the living God: when shall I come and appear before God?  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>My tears have been my meat day and night, while they continually say unto me, Where _is_ thy God?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>When I remember these _things_, I pour out my soul in me: for I had gone with the multitude, I went with them to the house of God, with the voice of joy and praise, with a multitude that kept holyday.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and _why_ art thou disquieted in me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him _for_ the help of his countenance.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ O my God, my soul is cast down within me: therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan, and of the Hermonites, from the hill Mizar.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Deep calleth unto deep at the noise of thy waterspouts: all thy waves and thy billows are gone over me.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>_Yet_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will command his lovingkindness in the daytime, and in the night his song _shall be_ with me, _and_ my prayer unto the God of my life.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I will say unto God my rock, Why hast thou forgotten me? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>_As_ with a sword in my bones, mine enemies reproach me; while they say daily unto me, Where _is_ thy God?  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him, _who is_ the health of my countenance, and my God.  

## PSALM 43.

Judge me, O God, and plead my cause against an ungodly nation: O deliver me from the deceitful and unjust man.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For thou _art_ the God of my strength: why dost thou cast me off? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>O send out thy light and thy truth: let them lead me; let them bring me unto thy holy hill, and to thy tabernacles.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Then will I go unto the altar of God, unto God my exceeding joy: yea, upon the harp will I praise thee, O God my God.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope in God: for I shall yet praise him, _who is_ the health of my countenance, and my God.  

## PSALM 44.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician for the sons of Korah, Maschil.</div>

We have heard with our ears, O God, our fathers have told us, _what_ work thou didst in their days, in the times of old.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>_How_ thou didst drive out the heathen with thy hand, and plantedst them; _how_ thou didst afflict the people, and cast them out.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For they got not the land in possession by their own sword, neither did their own arm save them: but thy right hand, and thine arm, and the light of thy countenance, because thou hadst a favour unto them.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thou art my King, O God: command deliverances for Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Through thee will we push down our enemies: through thy name will we tread them under that rise up against us.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>For I will not trust in my bow, neither shall my sword save me.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>But thou hast saved us from our enemies, and hast put them to shame that hated us.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>In God we boast all the day long, and praise thy name for ever. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ But thou hast cast off, and put us to shame; and goest not forth with our armies.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Thou makest us to turn back from the enemy: and they which hate us spoil for themselves.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Thou hast given us like sheep _appointed_ for meat; and hast scattered us among the heathen.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Thou sellest thy people for nought, and dost not increase _thy wealth_ by their price.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and a derision to them that are round about us.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Thou makest us a byword among the heathen, a shaking of the head among the people.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>My confusion _is_ continually before me, and the shame of my face hath covered me,  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>For the voice of him that reproacheth and blasphemeth; by reason of the enemy and avenger.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>¶ All this is come upon us; yet have we not forgotten thee, neither have we dealt falsely in thy covenant.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Our heart is not turned back, neither have our steps declined from thy way;  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Though thou hast sore broken us in the place of dragons, and covered us with the shadow of death.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>If we have forgotten the name of our God, or stretched out our hands to a strange god;  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Shall not God search this out? for he knoweth the secrets of the heart.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Yea, for thy sake are we killed all the day long; we are counted as sheep for the slaughter.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Awake, why sleepest thou, O Lord? arise, cast _us_ not off for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Wherefore hidest thou thy face, _and_ forgettest our affliction and our oppression?  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>For our soul is bowed down to the dust: our belly cleaveth unto the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>Arise for our help, and redeem us for thy mercies’ sake.  

## PSALM 45.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim, for the sons of Korah, Maschil, A Song of loves.</div>

My heart is inditing a good matter: I speak of the things which I have made touching the king: my tongue _is_ the pen of a ready writer.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thou art fairer than the children of men: grace is poured into thy lips: therefore God hath blessed thee for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Gird thy sword upon _thy_ thigh, O _most_ mighty, with thy glory and thy majesty.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>And in thy majesty ride prosperously because of truth and meekness _and_ righteousness; and thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thine arrows _are_ sharp in the heart of the king’s enemies; _whereby_ the people fall under thee.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Thy throne, O God, _is_ for ever and ever: the sceptre of thy kingdom _is_ a right sceptre.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Thou lovest righteousness, and hatest wickedness: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>All thy garments _smell_ of myrrh, and aloes, _and_ cassia, out of the ivory palaces, whereby they have made thee glad.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Kings’ daughters _were_ among thy honourable women: upon thy right hand did stand the queen in gold of Ophir.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ Hearken, O daughter, and consider, and incline thine ear; forget also thine own people, and thy father’s house;  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>So shall the king greatly desire thy beauty: for he _is_ thy Lord; and worship thou him.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>And the daughter of Tyre _shall be there_ with a gift; _even_ the rich among the people shall intreat thy favour.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>The king’s daughter _is_ all glorious within: her clothing _is_ of wrought gold.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>She shall be brought unto the king in raiment of needlework: the virgins her companions that follow her shall be brought unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>With gladness and rejoicing shall they be brought: they shall enter into the king’s palace.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Instead of thy fathers shall be thy children, whom thou mayest make princes in all the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>I will make thy name to be remembered in all generations: therefore shall the people praise thee for ever and ever.  

## PSALM 46.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician for the sons of Korah, A Song upon Alamoth.</div>

God _is_ our refuge and strength, a very present help in trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Therefore will not we fear, though the earth be removed, and though the mountains be carried into the midst of the sea;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>_Though_ the waters thereof roar _and_ be troubled, _though_ the mountains shake with the swelling thereof. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>_There is_ a river, the streams whereof shall make glad the city of God, the holy _place_ of the tabernacles of the most High.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>God _is_ in the midst of her; she shall not be moved: God shall help her, _and that_ right early.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ The heathen raged, the kingdoms were moved: he uttered his voice, the earth melted.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts _is_ with us; the God of Jacob _is_ our refuge. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Come, behold the works of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, what desolations he hath made in the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He maketh wars to cease unto the end of the earth; he breaketh the bow, and cutteth the spear in sunder; he burneth the chariot in the fire.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Be still, and know that I _am_ God: I will be exalted among the heathen, I will be exalted in the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts _is_ with us; the God of Jacob _is_ our refuge. Selah.  

## PSALM 47.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah.</div>

O clap your hands, all ye people; shout unto God with the voice of triumph.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> most high _is_ terrible; _he is_ a great King over all the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>He shall subdue the people under us, and the nations under our feet.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He shall choose our inheritance for us, the excellency of Jacob whom he loved. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ God is gone up with a shout, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with the sound of a trumpet.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Sing praises to God, sing praises: sing praises unto our King, sing praises.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>For God _is_ the King of all the earth: sing ye praises with understanding.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>God reigneth over the heathen: God sitteth upon the throne of his holiness.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The princes of the people are gathered together, _even_ the people of the God of Abraham: for the shields of the earth _belong_ unto God: he is greatly exalted.  

## PSALM 48.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song <em>and</em> Psalm for the sons of Korah.</div>

Great _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and greatly to be praised in the city of our God, _in_ the mountain of his holiness.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Beautiful for situation, the joy of the whole earth, _is_ mount Zion, _on_ the sides of the north, the city of the great King.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>God is known in her palaces for a refuge.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For, lo, the kings were assembled, they passed by together.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They saw _it, and_ so they marvelled; they were troubled, _and_ hasted away.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Fear took hold upon them there, _and_ pain, as of a woman in travail.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Thou breakest the ships of Tarshish with an east wind.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ As we have heard, so have we seen in the city of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts, in the city of our God: God will establish it for ever. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>We have thought of thy lovingkindness, O God, in the midst of thy temple.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>According to thy name, O God, so _is_ thy praise unto the ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Let mount Zion rejoice, let the daughters of Judah be glad, because of thy judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Walk about Zion, and go round about her: tell the towers thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Mark ye well her bulwarks, consider her palaces; that ye may tell _it_ to the generation following.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>For this God _is_ our God for ever and ever: he will be our guide _even_ unto death.  

## PSALM 49.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah.</div>

Hear this, all _ye_ people; give ear, all _ye_ inhabitants of the world:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Both low and high, rich and poor, together.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>My mouth shall speak of wisdom; and the meditation of my heart _shall be_ of understanding.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I will incline mine ear to a parable: I will open my dark saying upon the harp.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Wherefore should I fear in the days of evil, _when_ the iniquity of my heels shall compass me about?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ They that trust in their wealth, and boast themselves in the multitude of their riches;  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>None _of them_ can by any means redeem his brother, nor give to God a ransom for him:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>(For the redemption of their soul _is_ precious, and it ceaseth for ever:)  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>That he should still live for ever, _and_ not see corruption.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For he seeth _that_ wise men die, likewise the fool and the brutish person perish, and leave their wealth to others.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Their inward thought _is, that_ their houses _shall continue_ for ever, _and_ their dwelling places to all generations; they call _their_ lands after their own names.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Nevertheless man _being_ in honour abideth not: he is like the beasts _that_ perish.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>This their way _is_ their folly: yet their posterity approve their sayings. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Like sheep they are laid in the grave; death shall feed on them; and the upright shall have dominion over them in the morning; and their beauty shall consume in the grave from their dwelling.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>¶ But God will redeem my soul from the power of the grave: for he shall receive me. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Be not thou afraid when one is made rich, when the glory of his house is increased;  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>For when he dieth he shall carry nothing away: his glory shall not descend after him.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Though while he lived he blessed his soul: and _men_ will praise thee, when thou doest well to thyself.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>He shall go to the generation of his fathers; they shall never see light.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Man _that is_ in honour, and understandeth not, is like the beasts _that_ perish.  

## PSALM 50.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of Asaph.</div>

The mighty God, _even_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hath spoken, and called the earth from the rising of the sun unto the going down thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty, God hath shined.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Our God shall come, and shall not keep silence: a fire shall devour before him, and it shall be very tempestuous round about him.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He shall call to the heavens from above, and to the earth, that he may judge his people.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Gather my saints together unto me; those that have made a covenant with me by sacrifice.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>And the heavens shall declare his righteousness: for God _is_ judge himself. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Hear, O my people, and I will speak; O Israel, and I will testify against thee: I _am_ God, _even_ thy God.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I will not reprove thee for thy sacrifices or thy burnt offerings, _to have been_ continually before me.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I will take no bullock out of thy house, _nor_ he goats out of thy folds.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For every beast of the forest _is_ mine, _and_ the cattle upon a thousand hills.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>I know all the fowls of the mountains: and the wild beasts of the field _are_ mine.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>If I were hungry, I would not tell thee: for the world _is_ mine, and the fulness thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Will I eat the flesh of bulls, or drink the blood of goats?  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Offer unto God thanksgiving; and pay thy vows unto the most High:  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>And call upon me in the day of trouble: I will deliver thee, and thou shalt glorify me.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>¶ But unto the wicked God saith, What hast thou to do to declare my statutes, or _that_ thou shouldest take my covenant in thy mouth?  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Seeing thou hatest instruction, and castest my words behind thee.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>When thou sawest a thief, then thou consentedst with him, and hast been partaker with adulterers.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Thou givest thy mouth to evil, and thy tongue frameth deceit.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Thou sittest _and_ speakest against thy brother; thou slanderest thine own mother’s son.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>These _things_ hast thou done, and I kept silence; thou thoughtest that I was altogether _such an one_ as thyself: _but_ I will reprove thee, and set _them_ in order before thine eyes.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Now consider this, ye that forget God, lest I tear _you_ in pieces, and _there be_ none to deliver.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Whoso offereth praise glorifieth me: and to him that ordereth _his_ conversation _aright_ will I shew the salvation of God.  

## PSALM 51.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David, when Nathan the prophet came unto him, after he had gone in to Bath–sheba.</div>

Have mercy upon me, O God, according to thy lovingkindness: according unto the multitude of thy tender mercies blot out my transgressions.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Wash me throughly from mine iniquity, and cleanse me from my sin.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For I acknowledge my transgressions: and my sin _is_ ever before me.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Against thee, thee only, have I sinned, and done _this_ evil in thy sight: that thou mightest be justified when thou speakest, _and_ be clear when thou judgest.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Behold, I was shapen in iniquity; and in sin did my mother conceive me.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Behold, thou desirest truth in the inward parts: and in the hidden _part_ thou shalt make me to know wisdom.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Purge me with hyssop, and I shall be clean: wash me, and I shall be whiter than snow.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Make me to hear joy and gladness; _that_ the bones _which_ thou hast broken may rejoice.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Hide thy face from my sins, and blot out all mine iniquities.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Create in me a clean heart, O God; and renew a right spirit within me.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Cast me not away from thy presence; and take not thy holy spirit from me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Restore unto me the joy of thy salvation; and uphold me _with thy_ free spirit.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>_Then_ will I teach transgressors thy ways; and sinners shall be converted unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>¶ Deliver me from bloodguiltiness, O God, thou God of my salvation: _and_ my tongue shall sing aloud of thy righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>O Lord, open thou my lips; and my mouth shall shew forth thy praise.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>For thou desirest not sacrifice; else would I give _it_: thou delightest not in burnt offering.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The sacrifices of God _are_ a broken spirit: a broken and a contrite heart, O God, thou wilt not despise.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Do good in thy good pleasure unto Zion: build thou the walls of Jerusalem.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Then shalt thou be pleased with the sacrifices of righteousness, with burnt offering and whole burnt offering: then shall they offer bullocks upon thine altar.  

## PSALM 52.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, Maschil, <em>A Psalm</em> of David, when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, and said unto him, David is come to the house of Ahimelech.</div>

Why boastest thou thyself in mischief, O mighty man? the goodness of God _endureth_ continually.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thy tongue deviseth mischiefs; like a sharp razor, working deceitfully.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thou lovest evil more than good; _and_ lying rather than to speak righteousness. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thou lovest all devouring words, O _thou_ deceitful tongue.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>God shall likewise destroy thee for ever, he shall take thee away, and pluck thee out of _thy_ dwelling place, and root thee out of the land of the living. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ The righteous also shall see, and fear, and shall laugh at him:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Lo, _this is_ the man _that_ made not God his strength; but trusted in the abundance of his riches, _and_ strengthened himself in his wickedness.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>But I _am_ like a green olive tree in the house of God: I trust in the mercy of God for ever and ever.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I will praise thee for ever, because thou hast done _it_: and I will wait on thy name; for _it is_ good before thy saints.  

## PSALM 53.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Mahalath, Maschil, <em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

The fool hath said in his heart, _There is_ no God. Corrupt are they, and have done abominable iniquity: _there is_ none that doeth good.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>God looked down from heaven upon the children of men, to see if there were _any_ that did understand, that did seek God.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Every one of them is gone back: they are altogether become filthy; _there is_ none that doeth good, no, not one.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge? who eat up my people _as_ they eat bread: they have not called upon God.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>There were they in great fear, _where_ no fear was: for God hath scattered the bones of him that encampeth _against_ thee: thou hast put _them_ to shame, because God hath despised them.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Oh that the salvation of Israel _were come_ out of Zion! When God bringeth back the captivity of his people, Jacob shall rejoice, _and_ Israel shall be glad.  

## PSALM 54.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician on Neginoth, Maschil, <em>A Psalm</em> of David, when the Ziphims came and said to Saul, Doth not David hide himself with us?</div>

Save me, O God, by thy name, and judge me by thy strength.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Hear my prayer, O God; give ear to the words of my mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For strangers are risen up against me, and oppressors seek after my soul: they have not set God before them. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ Behold, God _is_ mine helper: the Lord _is_ with them that uphold my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>He shall reward evil unto mine enemies: cut them off in thy truth.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I will freely sacrifice unto thee: I will praise thy name, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for _it is_ good.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>For he hath delivered me out of all trouble: and mine eye hath seen _his desire_ upon mine enemies.  

## PSALM 55.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician on Neginoth, Maschil, <em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Give ear to my prayer, O God; and hide not thyself from my supplication.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Attend unto me, and hear me: I mourn in my complaint, and make a noise;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Because of the voice of the enemy, because of the oppression of the wicked: for they cast iniquity upon me, and in wrath they hate me.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>My heart is sore pained within me: and the terrors of death are fallen upon me.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Fearfulness and trembling are come upon me, and horror hath overwhelmed me.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>And I said, Oh that I had wings like a dove! _for then_ would I fly away, and be at rest.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Lo, _then_ would I wander far off, _and_ remain in the wilderness. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I would hasten my escape from the windy storm _and_ tempest.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ Destroy, O Lord, _and_ divide their tongues: for I have seen violence and strife in the city.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Day and night they go about it upon the walls thereof: mischief also and sorrow _are_ in the midst of it.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Wickedness _is_ in the midst thereof: deceit and guile depart not from her streets.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>For _it was_ not an enemy _that_ reproached me; then I could have borne _it_: neither _was it_ he that hated me _that_ did magnify _himself_ against me; then I would have hid myself from him:  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>But _it was_ thou, a man mine equal, my guide, and mine acquaintance.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>We took sweet counsel together, _and_ walked unto the house of God in company.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Let death seize upon them, _and_ let them go down quick into hell: for wickedness _is_ in their dwellings, _and_ among them.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>¶ As for me, I will call upon God; and the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall save me.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Evening, and morning, and at noon, will I pray, and cry aloud: and he shall hear my voice.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>He hath delivered my soul in peace from the battle _that was_ against me: for there were many with me.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>God shall hear, and afflict them, even he that abideth of old. Selah. Because they have no changes, therefore they fear not God.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>He hath put forth his hands against such as be at peace with him: he hath broken his covenant.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>_The words_ of his mouth were smoother than butter, but war _was_ in his heart: his words were softer than oil, yet _were_ they drawn swords.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Cast thy burden upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and he shall sustain thee: he shall never suffer the righteous to be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>But thou, O God, shalt bring them down into the pit of destruction: bloody and deceitful men shall not live out half their days; but I will trust in thee.  

## PSALM 56.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Jonath–elem–rechokim, Michtam of David, when the Philistines took him in Gath.</div>

Be merciful unto me, O God: for man would swallow me up; he fighting daily oppresseth me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Mine enemies would daily swallow _me_ up: for _they be_ many that fight against me, O thou most High.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>What time I am afraid, I will trust in thee.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>In God I will praise his word, in God I have put my trust; I will not fear what flesh can do unto me.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Every day they wrest my words: all their thoughts _are_ against me for evil.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>They gather themselves together, they hide themselves, they mark my steps, when they wait for my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Shall they escape by iniquity? in _thine_ anger cast down the people, O God.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Thou tellest my wanderings: put thou my tears into thy bottle: _are they_ not in thy book?  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>When I cry _unto thee_, then shall mine enemies turn back: this I know; for God _is_ for me.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>In God will I praise _his_ word: in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will I praise _his_ word.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>In God have I put my trust: I will not be afraid what man can do unto me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Thy vows _are_ upon me, O God: I will render praises unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>For thou hast delivered my soul from death: _wilt_ not _thou deliver_ my feet from falling, that I may walk before God in the light of the living?  

## PSALM 57.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, Al–taschith, Michtam of David, when he fled from Saul in the cave.</div>

Be merciful unto me, O God, be merciful unto me: for my soul trusteth in thee: yea, in the shadow of thy wings will I make my refuge, until _these_ calamities be overpast.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I will cry unto God most high; unto God that performeth _all things_ for me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>He shall send from heaven, and save me _from_ the reproach of him that would swallow me up. Selah. God shall send forth his mercy and his truth.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>My soul _is_ among lions: _and_ I lie _even among_ them that are set on fire, _even_ the sons of men, whose teeth _are_ spears and arrows, and their tongue a sharp sword.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens; _let_ thy glory _be_ above all the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>They have prepared a net for my steps; my soul is bowed down: they have digged a pit before me, into the midst whereof they are fallen _themselves_. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ My heart is fixed, O God, my heart is fixed: I will sing and give praise.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Awake up, my glory; awake, psaltery and harp: I _myself_ will awake early.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I will praise thee, O Lord, among the people: I will sing unto thee among the nations.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For thy mercy _is_ great unto the heavens, and thy truth unto the clouds.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: _let_ thy glory _be_ above all the earth.  

## PSALM 58.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, Al–taschith, Michtam of David.</div>

Do ye indeed speak righteousness, O congregation? do ye judge uprightly, O ye sons of men?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Yea, in heart ye work wickedness; ye weigh the violence of your hands in the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The wicked are estranged from the womb: they go astray as soon as they be born, speaking lies.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Their poison _is_ like the poison of a serpent: _they are_ like the deaf adder _that_ stoppeth her ear;  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Which will not hearken to the voice of charmers, charming never so wisely.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Break their teeth, O God, in their mouth: break out the great teeth of the young lions, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Let them melt away as waters _which_ run continually: _when_ he bendeth _his bow to shoot_ his arrows, let them be as cut in pieces.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>As a snail _which_ melteth, let _every one of them_ pass away: _like_ the untimely birth of a woman, _that_ they may not see the sun.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Before your pots can feel the thorns, he shall take them away as with a whirlwind, both living, and in _his_ wrath.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The righteous shall rejoice when he seeth the vengeance: he shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>So that a man shall say, Verily _there is_ a reward for the righteous: verily he is a God that judgeth in the earth.  

## PSALM 59.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, Al–taschith, Michtam of David; when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him.</div>

Deliver me from mine enemies, O my God: defend me from them that rise up against me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Deliver me from the workers of iniquity, and save me from bloody men.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For, lo, they lie in wait for my soul: the mighty are gathered against me; not _for_ my transgression, nor _for_ my sin, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>They run and prepare themselves without _my_ fault: awake to help me, and behold.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou therefore, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of hosts, the God of Israel, awake to visit all the heathen: be not merciful to any wicked transgressors. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>They return at evening: they make a noise like a dog, and go round about the city.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Behold, they belch out with their mouth: swords _are_ in their lips: for who, _say they_, doth hear?  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ But thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, shalt laugh at them; thou shalt have all the heathen in derision.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>_Because of_ his strength will I wait upon thee: for God _is_ my defence.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The God of my mercy shall prevent me: God shall let me see _my desire_ upon mine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Slay them not, lest my people forget: scatter them by thy power; and bring them down, O Lord our shield.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>_For_ the sin of their mouth _and_ the words of their lips let them even be taken in their pride: and for cursing and lying _which_ they speak.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Consume _them_ in wrath, consume _them_, that they _may_ not _be_: and let them know that God ruleth in Jacob unto the ends of the earth. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>And at evening let them return; _and_ let them make a noise like a dog, and go round about the city.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Let them wander up and down for meat, and grudge if they be not satisfied.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>But I will sing of thy power; yea, I will sing aloud of thy mercy in the morning: for thou hast been my defence and refuge in the day of my trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Unto thee, O my strength, will I sing: for God _is_ my defence, _and_ the God of my mercy.  

## PSALM 60.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Shushan–eduth, Michtam of David, to teach; when he strove with Aram–naharaim and with Aram–zobah, when Joab returned, and smote of Edom in the valley of salt twelve thousand.</div>

O God, thou hast cast us off, thou hast scattered us, thou hast been displeased; O turn thyself to us again.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thou hast made the earth to tremble; thou hast broken it: heal the breaches thereof; for it shaketh.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thou hast shewed thy people hard things: thou hast made us to drink the wine of astonishment.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thou hast given a banner to them that fear thee, that it may be displayed because of the truth. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>That thy beloved may be delivered; save _with_ thy right hand, and hear me.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Gilead _is_ mine, and Manasseh _is_ mine; Ephraim also _is_ the strength of mine head; Judah _is_ my lawgiver;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Moab _is_ my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe: Philistia, triumph thou because of me.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Who will bring me _into_ the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>_Wilt_ not thou, O God, _which_ hadst cast us off? and _thou_, O God, _which_ didst not go out with our armies?  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Give us help from trouble: for vain _is_ the help of man.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Through God we shall do valiantly: for he _it is that_ shall tread down our enemies.  

## PSALM 61.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Neginah, <em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Hear my cry, O God; attend unto my prayer.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>From the end of the earth will I cry unto thee, when my heart is overwhelmed: lead me to the rock _that_ is higher than I.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For thou hast been a shelter for me, _and_ a strong tower from the enemy.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I will abide in thy tabernacle for ever: I will trust in the covert of thy wings. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ For thou, O God, hast heard my vows: thou hast given _me_ the heritage of those that fear thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thou wilt prolong the king’s life: _and_ his years as many generations.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He shall abide before God for ever: O prepare mercy and truth, _which_ may preserve him.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>So will I sing praise unto thy name for ever, that I may daily perform my vows.  

## PSALM 62.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of David.</div>

Truly my soul waiteth upon God: from him _cometh_ my salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>He only _is_ my rock and my salvation; _he is_ my defence; I shall not be greatly moved.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>How long will ye imagine mischief against a man? ye shall be slain all of you: as a bowing wall _shall ye be, and as_ a tottering fence.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>They only consult to cast _him_ down from his excellency: they delight in lies: they bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>My soul, wait thou only upon God; for my expectation _is_ from him.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He only _is_ my rock and my salvation: _he is_ my defence; I shall not be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>In God _is_ my salvation and my glory: the rock of my strength, _and_ my refuge, _is_ in God.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Trust in him at all times; _ye_ people, pour out your heart before him: God _is_ a refuge for us. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Surely men of low degree _are_ vanity, _and_ men of high degree _are_ a lie: to be laid in the balance, they _are_ altogether _lighter_ than vanity.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Trust not in oppression, and become not vain in robbery: if riches increase, set not your heart _upon them_.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>God hath spoken once; twice have I heard this; that power _belongeth_ unto God.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Also unto thee, O Lord, _belongeth_ mercy: for thou renderest to every man according to his work.  

## PSALM 63.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David, when he was in the wilderness of Judah.</div>

O God, thou _art_ my God; early will I seek thee: my soul thirsteth for thee, my flesh longeth for thee in a dry and thirsty land, where no water is;  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>To see thy power and thy glory, so _as_ I have seen thee in the sanctuary.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>¶ Because thy lovingkindness _is_ better than life, my lips shall praise thee.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thus will I bless thee while I live: I will lift up my hands in thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>My soul shall be satisfied as _with_ marrow and fatness; and my mouth shall praise _thee_ with joyful lips:  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>When I remember thee upon my bed, _and_ meditate on thee in the _night_ watches.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Because thou hast been my help, therefore in the shadow of thy wings will I rejoice.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>My soul followeth hard after thee: thy right hand upholdeth me.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>But those _that_ seek my soul, to destroy _it_, shall go into the lower parts of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>They shall fall by the sword: they shall be a portion for foxes.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>But the king shall rejoice in God; every one that sweareth by him shall glory: but the mouth of them that speak lies shall be stopped.  

## PSALM 64.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

Hear my voice, O God, in my prayer: preserve my life from fear of the enemy.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Hide me from the secret counsel of the wicked; from the insurrection of the workers of iniquity:  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Who whet their tongue like a sword, _and_ bend _their bows to shoot_ their arrows, _even_ bitter words:  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>That they may shoot in secret at the perfect: suddenly do they shoot at him, and fear not.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They encourage themselves _in_ an evil matter: they commune of laying snares privily; they say, Who shall see them?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>They search out iniquities; they accomplish a diligent search: both the inward _thought_ of every one _of them_, and the heart, _is_ deep.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ But God shall shoot at them _with_ an arrow; suddenly shall they be wounded.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>So they shall make their own tongue to fall upon themselves: all that see them shall flee away.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>And all men shall fear, and shall declare the work of God; for they shall wisely consider of his doing.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The righteous shall be glad in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and shall trust in him; and all the upright in heart shall glory.  

## PSALM 65.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm <em>and</em> Song of David.</div>

Praise waiteth for thee, O God, in Sion: and unto thee shall the vow be performed.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>O thou that hearest prayer, unto thee shall all flesh come.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Iniquities prevail against me: _as for_ our transgressions, thou shalt purge them away.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Blessed _is the man whom_ thou choosest, and causest to approach _unto thee, that_ he may dwell in thy courts: we shall be satisfied with the goodness of thy house, _even_ of thy holy temple.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>_By_ terrible things in righteousness wilt thou answer us, O God of our salvation; _who art_ the confidence of all the ends of the earth, and of them that are afar off _upon_ the sea:  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Which by his strength setteth fast the mountains; _being_ girded with power:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Which stilleth the noise of the seas, the noise of their waves, and the tumult of the people.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They also that dwell in the uttermost parts are afraid at thy tokens: thou makest the outgoings of the morning and evening to rejoice.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou visitest the earth, and waterest it: thou greatly enrichest it with the river of God, _which_ is full of water: thou preparest them corn, when thou hast so provided for it.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Thou waterest the ridges thereof abundantly: thou settlest the furrows thereof: thou makest it soft with showers: thou blessest the springing thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Thou crownest the year with thy goodness; and thy paths drop fatness.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>They drop _upon_ the pastures of the wilderness: and the little hills rejoice on every side.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>The pastures are clothed with flocks; the valleys also are covered over with corn; they shout for joy, they also sing.  

## PSALM 66.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Song <em>or</em> Psalm.</div>

Make a joyful noise unto God, all ye lands:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Sing forth the honour of his name: make his praise glorious.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Say unto God, How terrible _art thou in_ thy works! through the greatness of thy power shall thine enemies submit themselves unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>All the earth shall worship thee, and shall sing unto thee; they shall sing _to_ thy name. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Come and see the works of God: _he is_ terrible _in his_ doing toward the children of men.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He turned the sea into dry _land_: they went through the flood on foot: there did we rejoice in him.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He ruleth by his power for ever; his eyes behold the nations: let not the rebellious exalt themselves. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ O bless our God, ye people, and make the voice of his praise to be heard:  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Which holdeth our soul in life, and suffereth not our feet to be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For thou, O God, hast proved us: thou hast tried us, as silver is tried.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Thou broughtest us into the net; thou laidst affliction upon our loins.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Thou hast caused men to ride over our heads; we went through fire and through water: but thou broughtest us out into a wealthy _place_.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>¶ I will go into thy house with burnt offerings: I will pay thee my vows,  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Which my lips have uttered, and my mouth hath spoken, when I was in trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>I will offer unto thee burnt sacrifices of fatlings, with the incense of rams; I will offer bullocks with goats. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Come _and_ hear, all ye that fear God, and I will declare what he hath done for my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>I cried unto him with my mouth, and he was extolled with my tongue.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>If I regard iniquity in my heart, the Lord will not hear _me_:  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>_But_ verily God hath heard _me_; he hath attended to the voice of my prayer.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ God, which hath not turned away my prayer, nor his mercy from me.  

## PSALM 67.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm <em>or</em> Song.</div>

God be merciful unto us, and bless us; _and_ cause his face to shine upon us; Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>That thy way may be known upon earth, thy saving health among all nations.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let the people praise thee, O God; let all the people praise thee.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>O let the nations be glad and sing for joy: for thou shalt judge the people righteously, and govern the nations upon earth. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Let the people praise thee, O God; let all the people praise thee.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>_Then_ shall the earth yield her increase; _and_ God, _even_ our own God, shall bless us.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>God shall bless us; and all the ends of the earth shall fear him.  

## PSALM 68.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm <em>or</em> Song of David.</div>

Let God arise, let his enemies be scattered: let them also that hate him flee before him.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>As smoke is driven away, _so_ drive _them_ away: as wax melteth before the fire, _so_ let the wicked perish at the presence of God.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>But let the righteous be glad; let them rejoice before God: yea, let them exceedingly rejoice.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Sing unto God, sing praises to his name: extol him that rideth upon the heavens by his name <span class="small-caps">Jah</span>, and rejoice before him.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>A father of the fatherless, and a judge of the widows, _is_ God in his holy habitation.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>God setteth the solitary in families: he bringeth out those which are bound with chains: but the rebellious dwell in a dry _land_.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ O God, when thou wentest forth before thy people, when thou didst march through the wilderness; Selah:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The earth shook, the heavens also dropped at the presence of God: _even_ Sinai itself _was moved_ at the presence of God, the God of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou, O God, didst send a plentiful rain, whereby thou didst confirm thine inheritance, when it was weary.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Thy congregation hath dwelt therein: thou, O God, hast prepared of thy goodness for the poor.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The Lord gave the word: great _was_ the company of those that published _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Kings of armies did flee apace: and she that tarried at home divided the spoil.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Though ye have lien among the pots, _yet shall ye be as_ the wings of a dove covered with silver, and her feathers with yellow gold.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>When the Almighty scattered kings in it, it was _white_ as snow in Salmon.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>¶ The hill of God _is as_ the hill of Bashan; an high hill _as_ the hill of Bashan.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Why leap ye, ye high hills? _this is_ the hill _which_ God desireth to dwell in; yea, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will dwell _in it_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The chariots of God _are_ twenty thousand, _even_ thousands of angels: the Lord _is_ among them, _as in_ Sinai, in the holy _place_.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Thou hast ascended on high, thou hast led captivity captive: thou hast received gifts for men; yea, _for_ the rebellious also, that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God might dwell _among them_.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ the Lord, _who_ daily loadeth us _with benefits, even_ the God of our salvation. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>_He that is_ our God _is_ the God of salvation; and unto <span class="small-caps">God</span> the Lord _belong_ the issues from death.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>But God shall wound the head of his enemies, _and_ the hairy scalp of such an one as goeth on still in his trespasses.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>¶ The Lord said, I will bring again from Bashan, I will bring _my people_ again from the depths of the sea:  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>That thy foot may be dipped in the blood of _thine_ enemies, _and_ the tongue of thy dogs in the same.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>They have seen thy goings, O God; _even_ the goings of my God, my King, in the sanctuary.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>The singers went before, the players on instruments _followed_ after; among _them were_ the damsels playing with timbrels.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>Bless ye God in the congregations, _even_ the Lord, from the fountain of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>There _is_ little Benjamin _with_ their ruler, the princes of Judah _and_ their council, the princes of Zebulun, _and_ the princes of Naphtali.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>Thy God hath commanded thy strength: strengthen, O God, that which thou hast wrought for us.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>Because of thy temple at Jerusalem shall kings bring presents unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>Rebuke the company of spearmen, the multitude of the bulls, with the calves of the people, _till every one_ submit himself with pieces of silver: scatter thou the people _that_ delight in war.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>Princes shall come out of Egypt; Ethiopia shall soon stretch out her hands unto God.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>¶ Sing unto God, ye kingdoms of the earth; O sing praises unto the Lord; Selah:  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>To him that rideth upon the heavens of heavens, _which were_ of old; lo, he doth send out his voice, _and that_ a mighty voice.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>Ascribe ye strength unto God: his excellency _is_ over Israel, and his strength _is_ in the clouds.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>O God, _thou art_ terrible out of thy holy places: the God of Israel _is_ he that giveth strength and power unto _his_ people. Blessed _be_ God.  

## PSALM 69.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim, <em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Save me, O God; for the waters are come in unto _my_ soul.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I sink in deep mire, where _there is_ no standing: I am come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>I am weary of my crying: my throat is dried: mine eyes fail while I wait for my God.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>They that hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of mine head: they that would destroy me, _being_ mine enemies wrongfully, are mighty: then I restored _that_ which I took not away.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>O God, thou knowest my foolishness; and my sins are not hid from thee.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Let not them that wait on thee, O Lord <span class="small-caps">God</span> of hosts, be ashamed for my sake: let not those that seek thee be confounded for my sake, O God of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Because for thy sake I have borne reproach; shame hath covered my face.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I am become a stranger unto my brethren, and an alien unto my mother’s children.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For the zeal of thine house hath eaten me up; and the reproaches of them that reproached thee are fallen upon me.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>When I wept, _and chastened_ my soul with fasting, that was to my reproach.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>I made sackcloth also my garment; and I became a proverb to them.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>They that sit in the gate speak against me; and I _was_ the song of the drunkards.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>¶ But as for me, my prayer _is_ unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _in_ an acceptable time: O God, in the multitude of thy mercy hear me, in the truth of thy salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Deliver me out of the mire, and let me not sink: let me be delivered from them that hate me, and out of the deep waters.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Let not the waterflood overflow me, neither let the deep swallow me up, and let not the pit shut her mouth upon me.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Hear me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for thy lovingkindness _is_ good: turn unto me according to the multitude of thy tender mercies.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>And hide not thy face from thy servant; for I am in trouble: hear me speedily.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Draw nigh unto my soul, _and_ redeem it: deliver me because of mine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Thou hast known my reproach, and my shame, and my dishonour: mine adversaries _are_ all before thee.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Reproach hath broken my heart; and I am full of heaviness: and I looked _for some_ to take pity, but _there was_ none; and for comforters, but I found none.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>They gave me also gall for my meat; and in my thirst they gave me vinegar to drink.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>¶ Let their table become a snare before them: and _that which should have been_ for _their_ welfare, _let it become_ a trap.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Let their eyes be darkened, that they see not; and make their loins continually to shake.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Pour out thine indignation upon them, and let thy wrathful anger take hold of them.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Let their habitation be desolate; _and_ let none dwell in their tents.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>For they persecute _him_ whom thou hast smitten; and they talk to the grief of those whom thou hast wounded.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>Add iniquity unto their iniquity: and let them not come into thy righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>Let them be blotted out of the book of the living, and not be written with the righteous.
