<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>But I _am_ poor and sorrowful: let thy salvation, O God, set me up on high.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>¶ I will praise the name of God with a song, and will magnify him with thanksgiving.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>_This_ also shall please the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> better than an ox _or_ bullock that hath horns and hoofs.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>The humble shall see _this, and_ be glad: and your heart shall live that seek God.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> heareth the poor, and despiseth not his prisoners.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>Let the heaven and earth praise him, the seas, and every thing that moveth therein.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>For God will save Zion, and will build the cities of Judah: that they may dwell there, and have it in possession.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>The seed also of his servants shall inherit it: and they that love his name shall dwell therein.  

## PSALM 70.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, <em>A Psalm</em> of David, to bring to remembrance.</div>

_Make haste_, O God, to deliver me; make haste to help me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let them be ashamed and confounded that seek after my soul: let them be turned backward, and put to confusion, that desire my hurt.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let them be turned back for a reward of their shame that say, Aha, aha.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: and let such as love thy salvation say continually, Let God be magnified.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>But I _am_ poor and needy: make haste unto me, O God: thou _art_ my help and my deliverer; O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, make no tarrying.  

## PSALM 71.

In thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, do I put my trust: let me never be put to confusion.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Deliver me in thy righteousness, and cause me to escape: incline thine ear unto me, and save me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Be thou my strong habitation, whereunto I may continually resort: thou hast given commandment to save me; for thou _art_ my rock and my fortress.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Deliver me, O my God, out of the hand of the wicked, out of the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For thou _art_ my hope, O Lord <span class="small-caps">God</span>: _thou art_ my trust from my youth.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>By thee have I been holden up from the womb: thou art he that took me out of my mother’s bowels: my praise _shall be_ continually of thee.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>I am as a wonder unto many; but thou _art_ my strong refuge.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Let my mouth be filled _with_ thy praise _and with_ thy honour all the day.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Cast me not off in the time of old age; forsake me not when my strength faileth.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For mine enemies speak against me; and they that lay wait for my soul take counsel together,  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Saying, God hath forsaken him: persecute and take him; for _there is_ none to deliver _him_.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>O God, be not far from me: O my God, make haste for my help.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Let them be confounded _and_ consumed that are adversaries to my soul; let them be covered _with_ reproach and dishonour that seek my hurt.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>¶ But I will hope continually, and will yet praise thee more and more.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>My mouth shall shew forth thy righteousness _and_ thy salvation all the day; for I know not the numbers _thereof_.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>I will go in the strength of the Lord <span class="small-caps">God</span>: I will make mention of thy righteousness, _even_ of thine only.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>O God, thou hast taught me from my youth: and hitherto have I declared thy wondrous works.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Now also when I am old and grayheaded, O God, forsake me not; until I have shewed thy strength unto _this_ generation, _and_ thy power to every one _that_ is to come.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Thy righteousness also, O God, _is_ very high, who hast done great things: O God, who _is_ like unto thee!  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>_Thou_, which hast shewed me great and sore troubles, shalt quicken me again, and shalt bring me up again from the depths of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Thou shalt increase my greatness, and comfort me on every side.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>I will also praise thee with the psaltery, _even_ thy truth, O my God: unto thee will I sing with the harp, O thou Holy One of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>My lips shall greatly rejoice when I sing unto thee; and my soul, which thou hast redeemed.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>My tongue also shall talk of thy righteousness all the day long: for they are confounded, for they are brought unto shame, that seek my hurt.  

## PSALM 72.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> for Solomon.</div>

Give the king thy judgments, O God, and thy righteousness unto the king’s son.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>¶ He shall judge thy people with righteousness, and thy poor with judgment.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The mountains shall bring peace to the people, and the little hills, by righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He shall judge the poor of the people, he shall save the children of the needy, and shall break in pieces the oppressor.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They shall fear thee as long as the sun and moon endure, throughout all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He shall come down like rain upon the mown grass: as showers _that_ water the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>In his days shall the righteous flourish; and abundance of peace so long as the moon endureth.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>He shall have dominion also from sea to sea, and from the river unto the ends of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>They that dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him; and his enemies shall lick the dust.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The kings of Tarshish and of the isles shall bring presents: the kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Yea, all kings shall fall down before him: all nations shall serve him.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>For he shall deliver the needy when he crieth; the poor also, and _him_ that hath no helper.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>He shall spare the poor and needy, and shall save the souls of the needy.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>He shall redeem their soul from deceit and violence: and precious shall their blood be in his sight.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>And he shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba: prayer also shall be made for him continually; _and_ daily shall he be praised.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>There shall be an handful of corn in the earth upon the top of the mountains; the fruit thereof shall shake like Lebanon: and _they_ of the city shall flourish like grass of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>His name shall endure for ever: his name shall be continued as long as the sun: and _men_ shall be blessed in him: all nations shall call him blessed.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>¶ Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God, the God of Israel, who only doeth wondrous things.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>And blessed _be_ his glorious name for ever: and let the whole earth be filled _with_ his glory; Amen, and Amen.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>The prayers of David the son of Jesse are ended.  

### BOOK III.

## PSALM 73.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of Asaph.</div>

Truly God _is_ good to Israel, _even_ to such as are of a clean heart.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>But as for me, my feet were almost gone; my steps had well nigh slipped.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For I was envious at the foolish, _when_ I saw the prosperity of the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For _there are_ no bands in their death: but their strength _is_ firm.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They _are_ not in trouble _as other_ men; neither are they plagued like _other_ men.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Therefore pride compasseth them about as a chain; violence covereth them _as_ a garment.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Their eyes stand out with fatness: they have more than heart could wish.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They are corrupt, and speak wickedly _concerning_ oppression: they speak loftily.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>They set their mouth against the heavens, and their tongue walketh through the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Therefore his people return hither: and waters of a full _cup_ are wrung out to them.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>And they say, How doth God know? and is there knowledge in the most High?  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Behold, these _are_ the ungodly, who prosper in the world; they increase _in_ riches.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Verily I have cleansed my heart _in_ vain, and washed my hands in innocency.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>For all the day long have I been plagued, and chastened every morning.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>¶ If I say, I will speak thus; behold, I should offend _against_ the generation of thy children.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>When I thought to know this, it _was_ too painful for me;  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Until I went into the sanctuary of God; _then_ understood I their end.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Surely thou didst set them in slippery places: thou castedst them down into destruction.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>How are they _brought_ into desolation, as in a moment! they are utterly consumed with terrors.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>As a dream when _one_ awaketh; _so_, O Lord, when thou awakest, thou shalt despise their image.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>¶ Thus my heart was grieved, and I was pricked in my reins.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>So foolish _was_ I, and ignorant: I was _as_ a beast before thee.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Nevertheless I _am_ continually with thee: thou hast holden _me_ by my right hand.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Thou shalt guide me with thy counsel, and afterward receive me _to_ glory.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Whom have I in heaven _but thee_? and _there is_ none upon earth _that_ I desire beside thee.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>My flesh and my heart faileth: _but_ God _is_ the strength of my heart, and my portion for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>For, lo, they that are far from thee shall perish: thou hast destroyed all them that go a whoring from thee.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>But _it is_ good for me to draw near to God: I have put my trust in the Lord <span class="small-caps">God</span>, that I may declare all thy works.  

## PSALM 74.

<div class="psalm-title">Maschil of Asaph.</div>

O God, why hast thou cast _us_ off for ever? _why_ doth thine anger smoke against the sheep of thy pasture?  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Remember thy congregation, _which_ thou hast purchased of old; the rod of thine inheritance, _which_ thou hast redeemed; this mount Zion, wherein thou hast dwelt.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Lift up thy feet unto the perpetual desolations; _even_ all _that_ the enemy hath done wickedly in the sanctuary.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thine enemies roar in the midst of thy congregations; they set up their ensigns _for_ signs.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>_A man_ was famous according as he had lifted up axes upon the thick trees.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>But now they break down the carved work thereof at once with axes and hammers.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>They have cast fire into thy sanctuary, they have defiled _by casting down_ the dwelling place of thy name to the ground.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They said in their hearts, Let us destroy them together: they have burned up all the synagogues of God in the land.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>We see not our signs: _there is_ no more any prophet: neither _is there_ among us any that knoweth how long.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>O God, how long shall the adversary reproach? shall the enemy blaspheme thy name for ever?  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Why withdrawest thou thy hand, even thy right hand? pluck _it_ out of thy bosom.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ For God _is_ my King of old, working salvation in the midst of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thou didst divide the sea by thy strength: thou brakest the heads of the dragons in the waters.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Thou brakest the heads of leviathan in pieces, _and_ gavest him _to be_ meat to the people inhabiting the wilderness.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Thou didst cleave the fountain and the flood: thou driedst up mighty rivers.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The day _is_ thine, the night also _is_ thine: thou hast prepared the light and the sun.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Thou hast set all the borders of the earth: thou hast made summer and winter.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>¶ Remember this, _that_ the enemy hath reproached, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and _that_ the foolish people have blasphemed thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>O deliver not the soul of thy turtledove unto the multitude _of the wicked_: forget not the congregation of thy poor for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Have respect unto the covenant: for the dark places of the earth are full of the habitations of cruelty.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>O let not the oppressed return ashamed: let the poor and needy praise thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Arise, O God, plead thine own cause: remember how the foolish man reproacheth thee daily.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Forget not the voice of thine enemies: the tumult of those that rise up against thee increaseth continually.  

## PSALM 75.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, Al–taschith, A Psalm <em>or</em> Song of Asaph.</div>

Unto thee, O God, do we give thanks, _unto thee_ do we give thanks: for _that_ thy name is near thy wondrous works declare.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>When I shall receive the congregation I will judge uprightly.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The earth and all the inhabitants thereof are dissolved: I bear up the pillars of it. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I said unto the fools, Deal not foolishly: and to the wicked, Lift not up the horn:  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Lift not up your horn on high: speak _not with_ a stiff neck.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ For promotion _cometh_ neither from the east, nor from the west, nor from the south.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>But God _is_ the judge: he putteth down one, and setteth up another.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>For in the hand of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _there is_ a cup, and the wine is red; it is full of mixture; and he poureth out of the same: but the dregs thereof, all the wicked of the earth shall wring _them_ out, _and_ drink _them_.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>But I will declare for ever; I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>All the horns of the wicked also will I cut off; _but_ the horns of the righteous shall be exalted.  

## PSALM 76.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician on Neginoth, A Psalm <em>or</em> Song of Asaph.</div>

In Judah _is_ God known: his name _is_ great in Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>In Salem also is his tabernacle, and his dwelling place in Zion.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>There brake he the arrows of the bow, the shield, and the sword, and the battle. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thou _art_ more glorious _and_ excellent than the mountains of prey.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The stouthearted are spoiled, they have slept their sleep: and none of the men of might have found their hands.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>At thy rebuke, O God of Jacob, both the chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Thou, _even_ thou, _art_ to be feared: and who may stand in thy sight when once thou art angry?  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Thou didst cause judgment to be heard from heaven; the earth feared, and was still,  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>When God arose to judgment, to save all the meek of the earth. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Surely the wrath of man shall praise thee: the remainder of wrath shalt thou restrain.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Vow, and pay unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> your God: let all that be round about him bring presents unto him that ought to be feared.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>He shall cut off the spirit of princes: _he is_ terrible to the kings of the earth.  

## PSALM 77.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, to Jeduthun, A Psalm of Asaph.</div>

I cried unto God with my voice, _even_ unto God with my voice; and he gave ear unto me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord: my sore ran in the night, and ceased not: my soul refused to be comforted.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>I remembered God, and was troubled: I complained, and my spirit was overwhelmed. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thou holdest mine eyes waking: I am so troubled that I cannot speak.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I have considered the days of old, the years of ancient times.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I call to remembrance my song in the night: I commune with mine own heart: and my spirit made diligent search.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Will the Lord cast off for ever? and will he be favourable no more?  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Is his mercy clean gone for ever? doth _his_ promise fail for evermore?  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Hath God forgotten to be gracious? hath he in anger shut up his tender mercies? Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>And I said, This _is_ my infirmity: _but I will remember_ the years of the right hand of the most High.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ I will remember the works of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: surely I will remember thy wonders of old.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>I will meditate also of all thy work, and talk of thy doings.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thy way, O God, _is_ in the sanctuary: who _is so_ great a God as _our_ God?  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Thou _art_ the God that doest wonders: thou hast declared thy strength among the people.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Thou hast with _thine_ arm redeemed thy people, the sons of Jacob and Joseph. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The waters saw thee, O God, the waters saw thee; they were afraid: the depths also were troubled.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The clouds poured out water: the skies sent out a sound: thine arrows also went abroad.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>The voice of thy thunder _was_ in the heaven: the lightnings lightened the world: the earth trembled and shook.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Thy way _is_ in the sea, and thy path in the great waters, and thy footsteps are not known.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Thou leddest thy people like a flock by the hand of Moses and Aaron.  

## PSALM 78.

<div class="psalm-title">Maschil of Asaph.</div>

Give ear, O my people, _to_ my law: incline your ears to the words of my mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I will open my mouth in a parable: I will utter dark sayings of old:  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Which we have heard and known, and our fathers have told us.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>We will not hide _them_ from their children, shewing to the generation to come the praises of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and his strength, and his wonderful works that he hath done.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For he established a testimony in Jacob, and appointed a law in Israel, which he commanded our fathers, that they should make them known to their children:  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>That the generation to come might know _them, even_ the children _which_ should be born; _who_ should arise and declare _them_ to their children:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>That they might set their hope in God, and not forget the works of God, but keep his commandments:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>And might not be as their fathers, a stubborn and rebellious generation; a generation _that_ set not their heart aright, and whose spirit was not stedfast with God.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ The children of Ephraim, _being_ armed, _and_ carrying bows, turned back in the day of battle.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>They kept not the covenant of God, and refused to walk in his law;  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>And forgat his works, and his wonders that he had shewed them.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Marvellous things did he in the sight of their fathers, in the land of Egypt, _in_ the field of Zoan.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>He divided the sea, and caused them to pass through; and he made the waters to stand as an heap.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>In the daytime also he led them with a cloud, and all the night with a light of fire.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>He clave the rocks in the wilderness, and gave _them_ drink as _out of_ the great depths.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>He brought streams also out of the rock, and caused waters to run down like rivers.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>And they sinned yet more against him by provoking the most High in the wilderness.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>And they tempted God in their heart by asking meat for their lust.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Yea, they spake against God; they said, Can God furnish a table in the wilderness?  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Behold, he smote the rock, that the waters gushed out, and the streams overflowed; can he give bread also? can he provide flesh for his people?  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Therefore the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> heard _this_, and was wroth: so a fire was kindled against Jacob, and anger also came up against Israel;  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Because they believed not in God, and trusted not in his salvation:  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Though he had commanded the clouds from above, and opened the doors of heaven,  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>And had rained down manna upon them to eat, and had given them of the corn of heaven.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Man did eat angels’ food: he sent them meat to the full.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>He caused an east wind to blow in the heaven: and by his power he brought in the south wind.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>He rained flesh also upon them as dust, and feathered fowls like as the sand of the sea:  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>And he let _it_ fall in the midst of their camp, round about their habitations.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>So they did eat, and were well filled: for he gave them their own desire;  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>They were not estranged from their lust. But while their meat _was_ yet in their mouths,  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>The wrath of God came upon them, and slew the fattest of them, and smote down the chosen _men_ of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>For all this they sinned still, and believed not for his wondrous works.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>Therefore their days did he consume in vanity, and their years in trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>When he slew them, then they sought him: and they returned and enquired early after God.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>And they remembered that God _was_ their rock, and the high God their redeemer.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>Nevertheless they did flatter him with their mouth, and they lied unto him with their tongues.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>For their heart was not right with him, neither were they stedfast in his covenant.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>But he, _being_ full of compassion, forgave _their_ iniquity, and destroyed _them_ not: yea, many a time turned he his anger away, and did not stir up all his wrath.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>For he remembered that they _were but_ flesh; a wind that passeth away, and cometh not again.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>¶ How oft did they provoke him in the wilderness, _and_ grieve him in the desert!  
<span class="verse-number">41&ensp;</span>Yea, they turned back and tempted God, and limited the Holy One of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>They remembered not his hand, _nor_ the day when he delivered them from the enemy.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>How he had wrought his signs in Egypt, and his wonders in the field of Zoan:  
<span class="verse-number">44&ensp;</span>And had turned their rivers into blood; and their floods, that they could not drink.  
<span class="verse-number">45&ensp;</span>He sent divers sorts of flies among them, which devoured them; and frogs, which destroyed them.  
<span class="verse-number">46&ensp;</span>He gave also their increase unto the caterpiller, and their labour unto the locust.  
<span class="verse-number">47&ensp;</span>He destroyed their vines with hail, and their sycomore trees with frost.  
<span class="verse-number">48&ensp;</span>He gave up their cattle also to the hail, and their flocks to hot thunderbolts.  
<span class="verse-number">49&ensp;</span>He cast upon them the fierceness of his anger, wrath, and indignation, and trouble, by sending evil angels _among them_.  
<span class="verse-number">50&ensp;</span>He made a way to his anger; he spared not their soul from death, but gave their life over to the pestilence;  
<span class="verse-number">51&ensp;</span>And smote all the firstborn in Egypt; the chief of _their_ strength in the tabernacles of Ham:  
<span class="verse-number">52&ensp;</span>But made his own people to go forth like sheep, and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.  
<span class="verse-number">53&ensp;</span>And he led them on safely, so that they feared not: but the sea overwhelmed their enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">54&ensp;</span>And he brought them to the border of his sanctuary, _even to_ this mountain, _which_ his right hand had purchased.  
<span class="verse-number">55&ensp;</span>He cast out the heathen also before them, and divided them an inheritance by line, and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents.  
<span class="verse-number">56&ensp;</span>Yet they tempted and provoked the most high God, and kept not his testimonies:  
<span class="verse-number">57&ensp;</span>But turned back, and dealt unfaithfully like their fathers: they were turned aside like a deceitful bow.  
<span class="verse-number">58&ensp;</span>For they provoked him to anger with their high places, and moved him to jealousy with their graven images.  
<span class="verse-number">59&ensp;</span>When God heard _this_, he was wroth, and greatly abhorred Israel:  
<span class="verse-number">60&ensp;</span>So that he forsook the tabernacle of Shiloh, the tent _which_ he placed among men;  
<span class="verse-number">61&ensp;</span>And delivered his strength into captivity, and his glory into the enemy’s hand.  
<span class="verse-number">62&ensp;</span>He gave his people over also unto the sword; and was wroth with his inheritance.  
<span class="verse-number">63&ensp;</span>The fire consumed their young men; and their maidens were not given to marriage.  
<span class="verse-number">64&ensp;</span>Their priests fell by the sword; and their widows made no lamentation.  
<span class="verse-number">65&ensp;</span>Then the Lord awaked as one out of sleep, _and_ like a mighty man that shouteth by reason of wine.  
<span class="verse-number">66&ensp;</span>And he smote his enemies in the hinder parts: he put them to a perpetual reproach.  
<span class="verse-number">67&ensp;</span>Moreover he refused the tabernacle of Joseph, and chose not the tribe of Ephraim:  
<span class="verse-number">68&ensp;</span>But chose the tribe of Judah, the mount Zion which he loved.  
<span class="verse-number">69&ensp;</span>And he built his sanctuary like high _palaces_, like the earth which he hath established for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">70&ensp;</span>He chose David also his servant, and took him from the sheepfolds:  
<span class="verse-number">71&ensp;</span>From following the ewes great with young he brought him to feed Jacob his people, and Israel his inheritance.  
<span class="verse-number">72&ensp;</span>So he fed them according to the integrity of his heart; and guided them by the skilfulness of his hands.  

## PSALM 79.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of Asaph.</div>

O God, the heathen are come into thine inheritance; thy holy temple have they defiled; they have laid Jerusalem on heaps.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The dead bodies of thy servants have they given _to be_ meat unto the fowls of the heaven, the flesh of thy saints unto the beasts of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Their blood have they shed like water round about Jerusalem; and _there was_ none to bury _them_.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>We are become a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and derision to them that are round about us.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>How long, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? wilt thou be angry for ever? shall thy jealousy burn like fire?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Pour out thy wrath upon the heathen that have not known thee, and upon the kingdoms that have not called upon thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>For they have devoured Jacob, and laid waste his dwelling place.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>O remember not against us former iniquities: let thy tender mercies speedily prevent us: for we are brought very low.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Help us, O God of our salvation, for the glory of thy name: and deliver us, and purge away our sins, for thy name’s sake.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Wherefore should the heathen say, Where _is_ their God? let him be known among the heathen in our sight _by_ the revenging of the blood of thy servants _which is_ shed.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Let the sighing of the prisoner come before thee; according to the greatness of thy power preserve thou those that are appointed to die;  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>And render unto our neighbours sevenfold into their bosom their reproach, wherewith they have reproached thee, O Lord.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>So we thy people and sheep of thy pasture will give thee thanks for ever: we will shew forth thy praise to all generations.  

## PSALM 80.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Shoshannim–eduth, A Psalm of Asaph.</div>

Give ear, O Shepherd of Israel, thou that leadest Joseph like a flock; thou that dwellest _between_ the cherubims, shine forth.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh stir up thy strength, and come _and_ save us.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Turn us again, O God, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of hosts, how long wilt thou be angry against the prayer of thy people?  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou feedest them with the bread of tears; and givest them tears to drink in great measure.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thou makest us a strife unto our neighbours: and our enemies laugh among themselves.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Turn us again, O God of hosts, and cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Thou hast brought a vine out of Egypt: thou hast cast out the heathen, and planted it.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou preparedst _room_ before it, and didst cause it to take deep root, and it filled the land.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The hills were covered with the shadow of it, and the boughs thereof _were like_ the goodly cedars.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>She sent out her boughs unto the sea, and her branches unto the river.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Why hast thou _then_ broken down her hedges, so that all they which pass by the way do pluck her?  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>The boar out of the wood doth waste it, and the wild beast of the field doth devour it.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Return, we beseech thee, O God of hosts: look down from heaven, and behold, and visit this vine;  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>And the vineyard which thy right hand hath planted, and the branch _that_ thou madest strong for thyself.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>_It is_ burned with fire, _it is_ cut down: they perish at the rebuke of thy countenance.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Let thy hand be upon the man of thy right hand, upon the son of man _whom_ thou madest strong for thyself.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>So will not we go back from thee: quicken us, and we will call upon thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Turn us again, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of hosts, cause thy face to shine; and we shall be saved.  

## PSALM 81.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Gittith, <em>A Psalm</em> of Asaph.</div>

Sing aloud unto God our strength: make a joyful noise unto the God of Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Take a psalm, and bring hither the timbrel, the pleasant harp with the psaltery.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Blow up the trumpet in the new moon, in the time appointed, on our solemn feast day.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For this _was_ a statute for Israel, _and_ a law of the God of Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>This he ordained in Joseph _for_ a testimony, when he went out through the land of Egypt: _where_ I heard a language _that_ I understood not.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I removed his shoulder from the burden: his hands were delivered from the pots.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Thou calledst in trouble, and I delivered thee; I answered thee in the secret place of thunder: I proved thee at the waters of Meribah. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Hear, O my people, and I will testify unto thee: O Israel, if thou wilt hearken unto me;  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>There shall no strange god be in thee; neither shalt thou worship any strange god.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>I _am_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> thy God, which brought thee out of the land of Egypt: open thy mouth wide, and I will fill it.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>But my people would not hearken to my voice; and Israel would none of me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>So I gave them up unto their own hearts’ lust: _and_ they walked in their own counsels.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Oh that my people had hearkened unto me, _and_ Israel had walked in my ways!  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>I should soon have subdued their enemies, and turned my hand against their adversaries.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>The haters of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> should have submitted themselves unto him: but their time should have endured for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>He should have fed them also with the finest of the wheat: and with honey out of the rock should I have satisfied thee.  

## PSALM 82.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of Asaph.</div>

God standeth in the congregation of the mighty; he judgeth among the gods.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>How long will ye judge unjustly, and accept the persons of the wicked? Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Defend the poor and fatherless: do justice to the afflicted and needy.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Deliver the poor and needy: rid _them_ out of the hand of the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They know not, neither will they understand; they walk on in darkness: all the foundations of the earth are out of course.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ I have said, Ye _are_ gods; and all of you _are_ children of the most High.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>But ye shall die like men, and fall like one of the princes.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Arise, O God, judge the earth: for thou shalt inherit all nations.  

## PSALM 83.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song <em>or</em> Psalm of Asaph.</div>

Keep not thou silence, O God: hold not thy peace, and be not still, O God.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For, lo, thine enemies make a tumult: and they that hate thee have lifted up the head.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>They have taken crafty counsel against thy people, and consulted against thy hidden ones.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>They have said, Come, and let us cut them off from _being_ a nation; that the name of Israel may be no more in remembrance.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For they have consulted together with one consent: they are confederate against thee:  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The tabernacles of Edom, and the Ishmaelites; of Moab, and the Hagarenes;  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Gebal, and Ammon, and Amalek; the Philistines with the inhabitants of Tyre;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Assur also is joined with them: they have holpen the children of Lot. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ Do unto them as _unto_ the Midianites; as _to_ Sisera, as _to_ Jabin, at the brook of Kison:  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>_Which_ perished at Endor: they became _as_ dung for the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Make their nobles like Oreb, and like Zeeb: yea, all their princes as Zebah, and as Zalmunna:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Who said, Let us take to ourselves the houses of God in possession.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>O my God, make them like a wheel; as the stubble before the wind.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>As the fire burneth a wood, and as the flame setteth the mountains on fire;  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>So persecute them with thy tempest, and make them afraid with thy storm.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Fill their faces with shame; that they may seek thy name, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Let them be confounded and troubled for ever; yea, let them be put to shame, and perish:  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>That _men_ may know that thou, whose name alone _is_ <span class="small-caps">Jehovah</span>, _art_ the most high over all the earth.  

## PSALM 84.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician upon Gittith, A Psalm for the sons of Korah.</div>

How amiable _are_ thy tabernacles, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts!  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>My soul longeth, yea, even fainteth for the courts of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: my heart and my flesh crieth out for the living God.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Yea, the sparrow hath found an house, and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may lay her young, _even_ thine altars, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts, my King, and my God.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Blessed _are_ they that dwell in thy house: they will be still praising thee. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Blessed _is_ the man whose strength _is_ in thee; in whose heart _are_ the ways _of them_.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>_Who_ passing through the valley of Baca make it a well; the rain also filleth the pools.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>They go from strength to strength, _every one of them_ in Zion appeareth before God.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of hosts, hear my prayer: give ear, O God of Jacob. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Behold, O God our shield, and look upon the face of thine anointed.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For a day in thy courts _is_ better than a thousand. I had rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God, than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God _is_ a sun and shield: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will give grace and glory: no good _thing_ will he withhold from them that walk uprightly.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> of hosts, blessed _is_ the man that trusteth in thee.  

## PSALM 85.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm for the sons of Korah.</div>

<span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou hast been favourable unto thy land: thou hast brought back the captivity of Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thou hast forgiven the iniquity of thy people, thou hast covered all their sin. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thou hast taken away all thy wrath: thou hast turned _thyself_ from the fierceness of thine anger.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Turn us, O God of our salvation, and cause thine anger toward us to cease.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Wilt thou be angry with us for ever? wilt thou draw out thine anger to all generations?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Wilt thou not revive us again: that thy people may rejoice in thee?  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Shew us thy mercy, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and grant us thy salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ I will hear what God the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will speak: for he will speak peace unto his people, and to his saints: but let them not turn again to folly.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Surely his salvation _is_ nigh them that fear him; that glory may dwell in our land.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Mercy and truth are met together; righteousness and peace have kissed _each other_.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Truth shall spring out of the earth; and righteousness shall look down from heaven.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Yea, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall give _that which is_ good; and our land shall yield her increase.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Righteousness shall go before him; and shall set _us_ in the way of his steps.  

## PSALM 86.

<div class="psalm-title">A Prayer of David.</div>

Bow down thine ear, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hear me: for I _am_ poor and needy.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Preserve my soul; for I _am_ holy: O thou my God, save thy servant that trusteth in thee.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Be merciful unto me, O Lord: for I cry unto thee daily.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Rejoice the soul of thy servant: for unto thee, O Lord, do I lift up my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For thou, Lord, _art_ good, and ready to forgive; and plenteous in mercy unto all them that call upon thee.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Give ear, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, unto my prayer; and attend to the voice of my supplications.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>In the day of my trouble I will call upon thee: for thou wilt answer me.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Among the gods _there is_ none like unto thee, O Lord; neither _are there any works_ like unto thy works.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>All nations whom thou hast made shall come and worship before thee, O Lord; and shall glorify thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For thou _art_ great, and doest wondrous things: thou _art_ God alone.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Teach me thy way, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; I will walk in thy truth: unite my heart to fear thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>I will praise thee, O Lord my God, with all my heart: and I will glorify thy name for evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>For great _is_ thy mercy toward me: and thou hast delivered my soul from the lowest hell.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>O God, the proud are risen against me, and the assemblies of violent _men_ have sought after my soul; and have not set thee before them.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>But thou, O Lord, _art_ a God full of compassion, and gracious, longsuffering, and plenteous in mercy and truth.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>O turn unto me, and have mercy upon me; give thy strength unto thy servant, and save the son of thine handmaid.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Shew me a token for good; that they which hate me may see _it_, and be ashamed: because thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hast holpen me, and comforted me.  

## PSALM 87.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm <em>or</em> Song for the sons of Korah.</div>

His foundation _is_ in the holy mountains.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> loveth the gates of Zion more than all the dwellings of Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Glorious things are spoken of thee, O city of God. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ I will make mention of Rahab and Babylon to them that know me: behold Philistia, and Tyre, with Ethiopia; this _man_ was born there.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>And of Zion it shall be said, This and that man was born in her: and the highest himself shall establish her.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall count, when he writeth up the people, _that_ this _man_ was born there. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>As well the singers as the players on instruments _shall be there_: all my springs _are_ in thee.  

## PSALM 88.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song <em>or</em> Psalm for the sons of Korah, to the chief Musician upon Mahalath Leannoth, Maschil of Heman the Ezrahite.</div>

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of my salvation, I have cried day _and_ night before thee:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let my prayer come before thee: incline thine ear unto my cry;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For my soul is full of troubles: and my life draweth nigh unto the grave.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I am counted with them that go down into the pit: I am as a man _that hath_ no strength:  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Free among the dead, like the slain that lie in the grave, whom thou rememberest no more: and they are cut off from thy hand.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thou hast laid me in the lowest pit, in darkness, in the deeps.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Thy wrath lieth hard upon me, and thou hast afflicted _me_ with all thy waves. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Thou hast put away mine acquaintance far from me; thou hast made me an abomination unto them: _I am_ shut up, and I cannot come forth.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Mine eye mourneth by reason of affliction: <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, I have called daily upon thee, I have stretched out my hands unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ Wilt thou shew wonders to the dead? shall the dead arise _and_ praise thee? Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Shall thy lovingkindness be declared in the grave? _or_ thy faithfulness in destruction?  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Shall thy wonders be known in the dark? and thy righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>But unto thee have I cried, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and in the morning shall my prayer prevent thee.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, why castest thou off my soul? _why_ hidest thou thy face from me?  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>I _am_ afflicted and ready to die from _my_ youth up: _while_ I suffer thy terrors I am distracted.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Thy fierce wrath goeth over me; thy terrors have cut me off.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>They came round about me daily like water; they compassed me about together.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Lover and friend hast thou put far from me, _and_ mine acquaintance into darkness.  

## PSALM 89.

<div class="psalm-title">Maschil of Ethan the Ezrahite.</div>

I will sing of the mercies of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> for ever: with my mouth will I make known thy faithfulness to all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For I have said, Mercy shall be built up for ever: thy faithfulness shalt thou establish in the very heavens.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>I have made a covenant with my chosen, I have sworn unto David my servant,  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Thy seed will I establish for ever, and build up thy throne to all generations. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ And the heavens shall praise thy wonders, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: thy faithfulness also in the congregation of the saints.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>For who in the heaven can be compared unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? _who_ among the sons of the mighty can be likened unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>?  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>God is greatly to be feared in the assembly of the saints, and to be had in reverence of all _them that are_ about him.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of hosts, who _is_ a strong <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> like unto thee? or to thy faithfulness round about thee?  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou rulest the raging of the sea: when the waves thereof arise, thou stillest them.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Thou hast broken Rahab in pieces, as one that is slain; thou hast scattered thine enemies with thy strong arm.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The heavens _are_ thine, the earth also _is_ thine: _as for_ the world and the fulness thereof, thou hast founded them.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>The north and the south thou hast created them: Tabor and Hermon shall rejoice in thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thou hast a mighty arm: strong is thy hand, _and_ high is thy right hand.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Justice and judgment _are_ the habitation of thy throne: mercy and truth shall go before thy face.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>¶ Blessed _is_ the people that know the joyful sound: they shall walk, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, in the light of thy countenance.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>In thy name shall they rejoice all the day: and in thy righteousness shall they be exalted.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>For thou _art_ the glory of their strength: and in thy favour our horn shall be exalted.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ our defence; and the Holy One of Israel _is_ our king.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>¶ Then thou spakest in vision to thy holy one, and saidst, I have laid help upon _one that is_ mighty; I have exalted _one_ chosen out of the people.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>I have found David my servant; with my holy oil have I anointed him:  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>With whom my hand shall be established: mine arm also shall strengthen him.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>The enemy shall not exact upon him; nor the son of wickedness afflict him.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>And I will beat down his foes before his face, and plague them that hate him.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>But my faithfulness and my mercy _shall be_ with him: and in my name shall his horn be exalted.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>I will set his hand also in the sea, and his right hand in the rivers.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>He shall cry unto me, Thou _art_ my father, my God, and the rock of my salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>Also I will make him _my_ firstborn, higher than the kings of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>My mercy will I keep for him for evermore, and my covenant shall stand fast with him.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>His seed also will I make _to endure_ for ever, and his throne as the days of heaven.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>If his children forsake my law, and walk not in my judgments;  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>If they break my statutes, and keep not my commandments;  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>Then will I visit their transgression with the rod, and their iniquity with stripes.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>Nevertheless my lovingkindness will I not utterly take from him, nor suffer my faithfulness to fail.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>My covenant will I not break, nor alter the thing that is gone out of my lips.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>Once have I sworn by my holiness that I will not lie unto David.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>His seed shall endure for ever, and his throne as the sun before me.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>It shall be established for ever as the moon, and _as_ a faithful witness in heaven. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>¶ But thou hast cast off and abhorred, thou hast been wroth with thine anointed.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>Thou hast made void the covenant of thy servant: thou hast profaned his crown _by casting it_ to the ground.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>Thou hast broken down all his hedges; thou hast brought his strong holds to ruin.  
<span class="verse-number">41&ensp;</span>All that pass by the way spoil him: he is a reproach to his neighbours.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>Thou hast set up the right hand of his adversaries; thou hast made all his enemies to rejoice.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>Thou hast also turned the edge of his sword, and hast not made him to stand in the battle.  
<span class="verse-number">44&ensp;</span>Thou hast made his glory to cease, and cast his throne down to the ground.  
<span class="verse-number">45&ensp;</span>The days of his youth hast thou shortened: thou hast covered him with shame. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">46&ensp;</span>How long, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? wilt thou hide thyself for ever? shall thy wrath burn like fire?  
<span class="verse-number">47&ensp;</span>Remember how short my time is: wherefore hast thou made all men in vain?  
<span class="verse-number">48&ensp;</span>What man _is he that_ liveth, and shall not see death? shall he deliver his soul from the hand of the grave? Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">49&ensp;</span>Lord, where _are_ thy former lovingkindnesses, _which_ thou swarest unto David in thy truth?  
<span class="verse-number">50&ensp;</span>Remember, Lord, the reproach of thy servants; _how_ I do bear in my bosom _the reproach of_ all the mighty people;  
<span class="verse-number">51&ensp;</span>Wherewith thine enemies have reproached, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; wherewith they have reproached the footsteps of thine anointed.  
<span class="verse-number">52&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> for evermore. Amen, and Amen.  

### BOOK IV.

## PSALM 90.

<div class="psalm-title">A Prayer of Moses the man of God.</div>

Lord, thou hast been our dwelling place in all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Before the mountains were brought forth, or ever thou hadst formed the earth and the world, even from everlasting to everlasting, thou _art_ God.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thou turnest man to destruction; and sayest, Return, ye children of men.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For a thousand years in thy sight _are but_ as yesterday when it is past, and _as_ a watch in the night.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou carriest them away as with a flood; they are _as_ a sleep: in the morning _they are_ like grass _which_ groweth up.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>In the morning it flourisheth, and groweth up; in the evening it is cut down, and withereth.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ For we are consumed by thine anger, and by thy wrath are we troubled.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Thou hast set our iniquities before thee, our secret _sins_ in the light of thy countenance.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For all our days are passed away in thy wrath: we spend our years as a tale _that is told_.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The days of our years _are_ threescore years and ten; and if by reason of strength _they be_ fourscore years, yet _is_ their strength labour and sorrow; for it is soon cut off, and we fly away.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Who knoweth the power of thine anger? even according to thy fear, _so is_ thy wrath.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ So teach _us_ to number our days, that we may apply _our_ hearts unto wisdom.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Return, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, how long? and let it repent thee concerning thy servants.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>O satisfy us early with thy mercy; that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Make us glad according to the days _wherein_ thou hast afflicted us, _and_ the years _wherein_ we have seen evil.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Let thy work appear unto thy servants, and thy glory unto their children.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>And let the beauty of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God be upon us: and establish thou the work of our hands upon us; yea, the work of our hands establish thou it.  

## PSALM 91.

He that dwelleth in the secret place of the most High shall abide under the shadow of the Almighty.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I will say of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _He is_ my refuge and my fortress: my God; in him will I trust.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Surely he shall deliver thee from the snare of the fowler, _and_ from the noisome pestilence.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He shall cover thee with his feathers, and under his wings shalt thou trust: his truth _shall be thy_ shield and buckler.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou shalt not be afraid for the terror by night; _nor_ for the arrow _that_ flieth by day;  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>_Nor_ for the pestilence _that_ walketh in darkness; _nor_ for the destruction _that_ wasteth at noonday.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>A thousand shall fall at thy side, and ten thousand at thy right hand; _but_ it shall not come nigh thee.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Only with thine eyes shalt thou behold and see the reward of the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ Because thou hast made the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _which is_ my refuge, _even_ the most High, thy habitation;  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>There shall no evil befall thee, neither shall any plague come nigh thy dwelling.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>For he shall give his angels charge over thee, to keep thee in all thy ways.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>They shall bear thee up in _their_ hands, lest thou dash thy foot against a stone.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thou shalt tread upon the lion and adder: the young lion and the dragon shalt thou trample under feet.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Because he hath set his love upon me, therefore will I deliver him: I will set him on high, because he hath known my name.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>He shall call upon me, and I will answer him: I _will be_ with him in trouble; I will deliver him, and honour him.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>With long life will I satisfy him, and shew him my salvation.  

## PSALM 92.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm <em>or</em> Song for the sabbath day.</div>

_It is a_ good _thing_ to give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and to sing praises unto thy name, O most High:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>To shew forth thy lovingkindness in the morning, and thy faithfulness every night,  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Upon an instrument of ten strings, and upon the psaltery; upon the harp with a solemn sound.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hast made me glad through thy work: I will triumph in the works of thy hands.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, how great are thy works! _and_ thy thoughts are very deep.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>A brutish man knoweth not; neither doth a fool understand this.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ When the wicked spring as the grass, and when all the workers of iniquity do flourish; _it is_ that they shall be destroyed for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>But thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _art most_ high for evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For, lo, thine enemies, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, for, lo, thine enemies shall perish; all the workers of iniquity shall be scattered.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>But my horn shalt thou exalt like _the horn of_ an unicorn: I shall be anointed with fresh oil.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Mine eye also shall see _my desire_ on mine enemies, _and_ mine ears shall hear _my desire_ of the wicked that rise up against me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree: he shall grow like a cedar in Lebanon.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Those that be planted in the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall flourish in the courts of our God.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>They shall still bring forth fruit in old age; they shall be fat and flourishing;  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>To shew that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ upright: _he is_ my rock, and _there is_ no unrighteousness in him.  

## PSALM 93.

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> reigneth, he is clothed with majesty; the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> is clothed with strength, _wherewith_ he hath girded himself: the world also is stablished, that it cannot be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thy throne _is_ established of old: thou _art_ from everlasting.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The floods have lifted up, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, the floods have lifted up their voice; the floods lift up their waves.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> on high _is_ mightier than the noise of many waters, _yea, than_ the mighty waves of the sea.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thy testimonies are very sure: holiness becometh thine house, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, for ever.  

## PSALM 94.

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God, to whom vengeance belongeth; O God, to whom vengeance belongeth, shew thyself.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Lift up thyself, thou judge of the earth: render a reward to the proud.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, how long shall the wicked, how long shall the wicked triumph?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>_How long_ shall they utter _and_ speak hard things? _and_ all the workers of iniquity boast themselves?  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They break in pieces thy people, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and afflict thine heritage.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>They slay the widow and the stranger, and murder the fatherless.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Yet they say, The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall not see, neither shall the God of Jacob regard _it_.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Understand, ye brutish among the people: and _ye_ fools, when will ye be wise?  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He that planted the ear, shall he not hear? he that formed the eye, shall he not see?  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>He that chastiseth the heathen, shall not he correct? he that teacheth man knowledge, _shall not he know_?  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> knoweth the thoughts of man, that they _are_ vanity.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ Blessed _is_ the man whom thou chastenest, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and teachest him out of thy law;  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>That thou mayest give him rest from the days of adversity, until the pit be digged for the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will not cast off his people, neither will he forsake his inheritance.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>But judgment shall return unto righteousness: and all the upright in heart shall follow it.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Who will rise up for me against the evildoers? _or_ who will stand up for me against the workers of iniquity?  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Unless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _had been_ my help, my soul had almost dwelt in silence.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>When I said, My foot slippeth; thy mercy, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, held me up.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>In the multitude of my thoughts within me thy comforts delight my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Shall the throne of iniquity have fellowship with thee, which frameth mischief by a law?  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>They gather themselves together against the soul of the righteous, and condemn the innocent blood.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>But the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> is my defence; and my God _is_ the rock of my refuge.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>And he shall bring upon them their own iniquity, and shall cut them off in their own wickedness; _yea_, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God shall cut them off.  

## PSALM 95.

O come, let us sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: let us make a joyful noise to the rock of our salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let us come before his presence with thanksgiving, and make a joyful noise unto him with psalms.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ a great God, and a great King above all gods.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>In his hand _are_ the deep places of the earth: the strength of the hills _is_ his also.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The sea _is_ his, and he made it: and his hands formed the dry _land_.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>O come, let us worship and bow down: let us kneel before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our maker.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ For he _is_ our God; and we _are_ the people of his pasture, and the sheep of his hand. To day if ye will hear his voice,  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Harden not your heart, as in the provocation, _and_ as _in_ the day of temptation in the wilderness:  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>When your fathers tempted me, proved me, and saw my work.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Forty years long was I grieved with _this_ generation, and said, It _is_ a people that do err in their heart, and they have not known my ways:  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Unto whom I sware in my wrath that they should not enter into my rest.  

## PSALM 96.

O sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> a new song: sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, bless his name; shew forth his salvation from day to day.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Declare his glory among the heathen, his wonders among all people.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ great, and greatly to be praised: he _is_ to be feared above all gods.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For all the gods of the nations _are_ idols: but the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> made the heavens.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Honour and majesty _are_ before him: strength and beauty _are_ in his sanctuary.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Give unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O ye kindreds of the people, give unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> glory and strength.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Give unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> the glory _due unto_ his name: bring an offering, and come into his courts.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>O worship the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in the beauty of holiness: fear before him, all the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ Say among the heathen _that_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> reigneth: the world also shall be established that it shall not be moved: he shall judge the people righteously.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Let the heavens rejoice, and let the earth be glad; let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Let the field be joyful, and all that _is_ therein: then shall all the trees of the wood rejoice  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for he cometh, for he cometh to judge the earth: he shall judge the world with righteousness, and the people with his truth.  

## PSALM 97.

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> reigneth; let the earth rejoice; let the multitude of isles be glad _thereof_.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Clouds and darkness _are_ round about him: righteousness and judgment _are_ the habitation of his throne.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>A fire goeth before him, and burneth up his enemies round about.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>His lightnings enlightened the world: the earth saw, and trembled.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The hills melted like wax at the presence of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The heavens declare his righteousness, and all the people see his glory.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Confounded be all they that serve graven images, that boast themselves of idols: worship him, all _ye_ gods.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Zion heard, and was glad; and the daughters of Judah rejoiced because of thy judgments, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _art_ high above all the earth: thou art exalted far above all gods.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Ye that love the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hate evil: he preserveth the souls of his saints; he delivereth them out of the hand of the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Light is sown for the righteous, and gladness for the upright in heart.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Rejoice in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, ye righteous; and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.  

## PSALM 98.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm.</div>

O sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> a new song; for he hath done marvellous things: his right hand, and his holy arm, hath gotten him the victory.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath made known his salvation: his righteousness hath he openly shewed in the sight of the heathen.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>He hath remembered his mercy and his truth toward the house of Israel: all the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ Make a joyful noise unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all the earth: make a loud noise, and rejoice, and sing praise.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with the harp; with the harp, and the voice of a psalm.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>With trumpets and sound of cornet make a joyful noise before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, the King.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Let the sea roar, and the fulness thereof; the world, and they that dwell therein.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Let the floods clap _their_ hands: let the hills be joyful together  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for he cometh to judge the earth: with righteousness shall he judge the world, and the people with equity.  

## PSALM 99.

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> reigneth; let the people tremble: he sitteth _between_ the cherubims; let the earth be moved.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ great in Zion; and he _is_ high above all the people.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let them praise thy great and terrible name; _for_ it _is_ holy.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The king’s strength also loveth judgment; thou dost establish equity, thou executest judgment and righteousness in Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Exalt ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God, and worship at his footstool; _for_ he _is_ holy.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Moses and Aaron among his priests, and Samuel among them that call upon his name; they called upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and he answered them.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He spake unto them in the cloudy pillar: they kept his testimonies, and the ordinance _that_ he gave them.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Thou answeredst them, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God: thou wast a God that forgavest them, though thou tookest vengeance of their inventions.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Exalt the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God, and worship at his holy hill; for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God _is_ holy.  

## PSALM 100.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of praise.</div>

Make a joyful noise unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all ye lands.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Serve the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with gladness: come before his presence with singing.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Know ye that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> he _is_ God: _it is_ he _that_ hath made us, and not we ourselves; _we are_ his people, and the sheep of his pasture.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Enter into his gates with thanksgiving, _and_ into his courts with praise: be thankful unto him, _and_ bless his name.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ good; his mercy _is_ everlasting; and his truth _endureth_ to all generations.  

## PSALM 101.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

I will sing of mercy and judgment: unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, will I sing.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I will behave myself wisely in a perfect way. O when wilt thou come unto me? I will walk within my house with a perfect heart.
