<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>I will set no wicked thing before mine eyes: I hate the work of them that turn aside; _it_ shall not cleave to me.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>A froward heart shall depart from me: I will not know a wicked _person_.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Whoso privily slandereth his neighbour, him will I cut off: him that hath an high look and a proud heart will not I suffer.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Mine eyes _shall be_ upon the faithful of the land, that they may dwell with me: he that walketh in a perfect way, he shall serve me.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He that worketh deceit shall not dwell within my house: he that telleth lies shall not tarry in my sight.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I will early destroy all the wicked of the land; that I may cut off all wicked doers from the city of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 102.

<div class="psalm-title">A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed, and poureth out his complaint before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.</div>

Hear my prayer, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and let my cry come unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Hide not thy face from me in the day _when_ I am in trouble; incline thine ear unto me: in the day _when_ I call answer me speedily.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For my days are consumed like smoke, and my bones are burned as an hearth.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>My heart is smitten, and withered like grass; so that I forget to eat my bread.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>By reason of the voice of my groaning my bones cleave to my skin.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I am like a pelican of the wilderness: I am like an owl of the desert.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>I watch, and am as a sparrow alone upon the house top.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Mine enemies reproach me all the day; _and_ they that are mad against me are sworn against me.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For I have eaten ashes like bread, and mingled my drink with weeping,  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Because of thine indignation and thy wrath: for thou hast lifted me up, and cast me down.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>My days _are_ like a shadow that declineth; and I am withered like grass.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ But thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, shalt endure for ever; and thy remembrance unto all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thou shalt arise, _and_ have mercy upon Zion: for the time to favour her, yea, the set time, is come.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>For thy servants take pleasure in her stones, and favour the dust thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>So the heathen shall fear the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and all the kings of the earth thy glory.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>When the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall build up Zion, he shall appear in his glory.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>He will regard the prayer of the destitute, and not despise their prayer.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>This shall be written for the generation to come: and the people which shall be created shall praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>For he hath looked down from the height of his sanctuary; from heaven did the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> behold the earth;  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>To hear the groaning of the prisoner; to loose those that are appointed to death;  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>To declare the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in Zion, and his praise in Jerusalem;  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>When the people are gathered together, and the kingdoms, to serve the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>¶ He weakened my strength in the way; he shortened my days.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>I said, O my God, take me not away in the midst of my days: thy years _are_ throughout all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Of old hast thou laid the foundation of the earth: and the heavens _are_ the work of thy hands.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>They shall perish, but thou shalt endure: yea, all of them shall wax old like a garment; as a vesture shalt thou change them, and they shall be changed:  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>But thou _art_ the same, and thy years shall have no end.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>The children of thy servants shall continue, and their seed shall be established before thee.  

## PSALM 103.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O my soul: and all that is within me, _bless_ his holy name.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O my soul, and forget not all his benefits:  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Who forgiveth all thine iniquities; who healeth all thy diseases;  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Who redeemeth thy life from destruction; who crowneth thee with lovingkindness and tender mercies;  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Who satisfieth thy mouth with good _things; so that_ thy youth is renewed like the eagle’s.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> executeth righteousness and judgment for all that are oppressed.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He made known his ways unto Moses, his acts unto the children of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and plenteous in mercy.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He will not always chide: neither will he keep _his anger_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>He hath not dealt with us after our sins; nor rewarded us according to our iniquities.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>For as the heaven is high above the earth, _so_ great is his mercy toward them that fear him.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>As far as the east is from the west, _so_ far hath he removed our transgressions from us.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Like as a father pitieth _his_ children, _so_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> pitieth them that fear him.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>For he knoweth our frame; he remembereth that we _are_ dust.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>_As for_ man, his days _are_ as grass: as a flower of the field, so he flourisheth.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone; and the place thereof shall know it no more.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>But the mercy of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ from everlasting to everlasting upon them that fear him, and his righteousness unto children’s children;  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>To such as keep his covenant, and to those that remember his commandments to do them.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>¶ The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath prepared his throne in the heavens; and his kingdom ruleth over all.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, ye his angels, that excel in strength, that do his commandments, hearkening unto the voice of his word.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Bless ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all _ye_ his hosts; _ye_ ministers of his, that do his pleasure.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all his works in all places of his dominion: bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O my soul.  

## PSALM 104.

Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O my soul. O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God, thou art very great; thou art clothed with honour and majesty.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Who coverest _thyself_ with light as _with_ a garment: who stretchest out the heavens like a curtain:  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Who layeth the beams of his chambers in the waters: who maketh the clouds his chariot: who walketh upon the wings of the wind:  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Who maketh his angels spirits; his ministers a flaming fire:  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>_Who_ laid the foundations of the earth, _that_ it should not be removed for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Thou coveredst it with the deep as _with_ a garment: the waters stood above the mountains.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>At thy rebuke they fled; at the voice of thy thunder they hasted away.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They go up by the mountains; they go down by the valleys unto the place which thou hast founded for them.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Thou hast set a bound that they may not pass over; that they turn not again to cover the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ He sendeth the springs into the valleys, _which_ run among the hills.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>They give drink to every beast of the field: the wild asses quench their thirst.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>By them shall the fowls of the heaven have their habitation, _which_ sing among the branches.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>He watereth the hills from his chambers: the earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>He causeth the grass to grow for the cattle, and herb for the service of man: that he may bring forth food out of the earth;  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>And wine _that_ maketh glad the heart of man, _and_ oil to make _his_ face to shine, and bread _which_ strengtheneth man’s heart.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The trees of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> are full _of sap_; the cedars of Lebanon, which he hath planted;  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>Where the birds make their nests: _as for_ the stork, the fir trees _are_ her house.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>The high hills _are_ a refuge for the wild goats; _and_ the rocks for the conies.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>¶ He appointed the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Thou makest darkness, and it is night: wherein all the beasts of the forest do creep _forth_.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>The young lions roar after their prey, and seek their meat from God.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>The sun ariseth, they gather themselves together, and lay them down in their dens.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Man goeth forth unto his work and to his labour until the evening.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, how manifold are thy works! in wisdom hast thou made them all: the earth is full of thy riches.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>_So is_ this great and wide sea, wherein _are_ things creeping innumerable, both small and great beasts.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>There go the ships: _there is_ that leviathan, _whom_ thou hast made to play therein.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>These wait all upon thee; that thou mayest give _them_ their meat in due season.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>_That_ thou givest them they gather: thou openest thine hand, they are filled with good.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled: thou takest away their breath, they die, and return to their dust.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created: and thou renewest the face of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>¶ The glory of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall endure for ever: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall rejoice in his works.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>He looketh on the earth, and it trembleth: he toucheth the hills, and they smoke.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>I will sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>My meditation of him shall be sweet: I will be glad in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>Let the sinners be consumed out of the earth, and let the wicked be no more. Bless thou the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O my soul. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 105.

O give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; call upon his name: make known his deeds among the people.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Sing unto him, sing psalms unto him: talk ye of all his wondrous works.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Seek the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and his strength: seek his face evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Remember his marvellous works that he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth;  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>O ye seed of Abraham his servant, ye children of Jacob his chosen.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God: his judgments _are_ in all the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ He hath remembered his covenant for ever, the word _which_ he commanded to a thousand generations.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Which _covenant_ he made with Abraham, and his oath unto Isaac;  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>And confirmed the same unto Jacob for a law, _and_ to Israel _for_ an everlasting covenant:  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Saying, Unto thee will I give the land of Canaan, the lot of your inheritance:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>When they were _but_ a few men in number; yea, very few, and strangers in it.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>When they went from one nation to another, from _one_ kingdom to another people;  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>He suffered no man to do them wrong: yea, he reproved kings for their sakes;  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>_Saying_, Touch not mine anointed, and do my prophets no harm.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Moreover he called for a famine upon the land: he brake the whole staff of bread.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>He sent a man before them, _even_ Joseph, _who_ was sold for a servant:  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Whose feet they hurt with fetters: he was laid in iron:  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Until the time that his word came: the word of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> tried him.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>The king sent and loosed him; _even_ the ruler of the people, and let him go free.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>He made him lord of his house, and ruler of all his substance:  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>To bind his princes at his pleasure; and teach his senators wisdom.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Israel also came into Egypt; and Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>And he increased his people greatly; and made them stronger than their enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>¶ He turned their heart to hate his people, to deal subtilly with his servants.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>He sent Moses his servant; _and_ Aaron whom he had chosen.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>They shewed his signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>He sent darkness, and made it dark; and they rebelled not against his word.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>He turned their waters into blood, and slew their fish.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>Their land brought forth frogs in abundance, in the chambers of their kings.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>He spake, and there came divers sorts of flies, _and_ lice in all their coasts.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>He gave them hail for rain, _and_ flaming fire in their land.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>He smote their vines also and their fig trees; and brake the trees of their coasts.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>He spake, and the locusts came, and caterpillers, and that without number,  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>And did eat up all the herbs in their land, and devoured the fruit of their ground.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>He smote also all the firstborn in their land, the chief of all their strength.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>He brought them forth also with silver and gold: and _there was_ not one feeble _person_ among their tribes.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them fell upon them.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>He spread a cloud for a covering; and fire to give light in the night.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>_The people_ asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them with the bread of heaven.  
<span class="verse-number">41&ensp;</span>He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out; they ran in the dry places _like_ a river.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>For he remembered his holy promise, _and_ Abraham his servant.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>And he brought forth his people with joy, _and_ his chosen with gladness:  
<span class="verse-number">44&ensp;</span>And gave them the lands of the heathen: and they inherited the labour of the people;  
<span class="verse-number">45&ensp;</span>That they might observe his statutes, and keep his laws. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 106.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. O give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for _he is_ good: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Who can utter the mighty acts of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>? _who_ can shew forth all his praise?  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Blessed _are_ they that keep judgment, _and_ he that doeth righteousness at all times.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Remember me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, with the favour _that thou bearest unto_ thy people: O visit me with thy salvation;  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>That I may see the good of thy chosen, that I may rejoice in the gladness of thy nation, that I may glory with thine inheritance.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ We have sinned with our fathers, we have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt; they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies; but provoked _him_ at the sea, _even_ at the Red sea.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Nevertheless he saved them for his name’s sake, that he might make his mighty power to be known.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He rebuked the Red sea also, and it was dried up: so he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>And he saved them from the hand of him that hated _them_, and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>And the waters covered their enemies: there was not one of them left.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Then believed they his words; they sang his praise.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>¶ They soon forgat his works; they waited not for his counsel:  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, and tempted God in the desert.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>And he gave them their request; but sent leanness into their soul.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>They envied Moses also in the camp, _and_ Aaron the saint of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan, and covered the company of Abiram.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>And a fire was kindled in their company; the flame burned up the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>They made a calf in Horeb, and worshipped the molten image.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Thus they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox that eateth grass.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>They forgat God their saviour, which had done great things in Egypt;  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Wondrous works in the land of Ham, _and_ terrible things by the Red sea.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy _them_.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Yea, they despised the pleasant land, they believed not his word:  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>But murmured in their tents, _and_ hearkened not unto the voice of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, to overthrow them in the wilderness:  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>To overthrow their seed also among the nations, and to scatter them in the lands.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>They joined themselves also unto Baal–peor, and ate the sacrifices of the dead.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>Thus they provoked _him_ to anger with their inventions: and the plague brake in upon them.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: and _so_ the plague was stayed.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>And that was counted unto him for righteousness unto all generations for evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>They angered _him_ also at the waters of strife, so that it went ill with Moses for their sakes:  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>Because they provoked his spirit, so that he spake unadvisedly with his lips.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>¶ They did not destroy the nations, concerning whom the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> commanded them:  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>And they served their idols: which were a snare unto them.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>Yea, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto devils,  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>And shed innocent blood, _even_ the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan: and the land was polluted with blood.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>Thus were they defiled with their own works, and went a whoring with their own inventions.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>Therefore was the wrath of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> kindled against his people, insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance.  
<span class="verse-number">41&ensp;</span>And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; and they that hated them ruled over them.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>Their enemies also oppressed them, and they were brought into subjection under their hand.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>Many times did he deliver them; but they provoked _him_ with their counsel, and were brought low for their iniquity.  
<span class="verse-number">44&ensp;</span>Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, when he heard their cry:  
<span class="verse-number">45&ensp;</span>And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.  
<span class="verse-number">46&ensp;</span>He made them also to be pitied of all those that carried them captives.  
<span class="verse-number">47&ensp;</span>Save us, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God, and gather us from among the heathen, to give thanks unto thy holy name, _and_ to triumph in thy praise.  
<span class="verse-number">48&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> God of Israel from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

### BOOK V.

## PSALM 107.

O give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, for _he is_ good: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let the redeemed of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> say _so_, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>And gathered them out of the lands, from the east, and from the west, from the north, and from the south.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; they found no city to dwell in.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Then they cried unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in their trouble, _and_ he delivered them out of their distresses.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>And he led them forth by the right way, that they might go to a city of habitation.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Oh that _men_ would praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _for_ his goodness, and _for_ his wonderful works to the children of men!  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>For he satisfieth the longing soul, and filleth the hungry soul with goodness.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ Such as sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, _being_ bound in affliction and iron;  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Because they rebelled against the words of God, and contemned the counsel of the most High:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Therefore he brought down their heart with labour; they fell down, and _there was_ none to help.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Then they cried unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in their trouble, _and_ he saved them out of their distresses.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, and brake their bands in sunder.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Oh that _men_ would praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _for_ his goodness, and _for_ his wonderful works to the children of men!  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>For he hath broken the gates of brass, and cut the bars of iron in sunder.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>¶ Fools because of their transgression, and because of their iniquities, are afflicted.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Their soul abhorreth all manner of meat; and they draw near unto the gates of death.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Then they cry unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in their trouble, _and_ he saveth them out of their distresses.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>He sent his word, and healed them, and delivered _them_ from their destructions.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Oh that _men_ would praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _for_ his goodness, and _for_ his wonderful works to the children of men!  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and declare his works with rejoicing.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>¶ They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business in great waters;  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>These see the works of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and his wonders in the deep.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, which lifteth up the waves thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths: their soul is melted because of trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and are at their wits’ end.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>Then they cry unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in their trouble, and he bringeth them out of their distresses.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>He maketh the storm a calm, so that the waves thereof are still.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>Then are they glad because they be quiet; so he bringeth them unto their desired haven.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>Oh that _men_ would praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _for_ his goodness, and _for_ his wonderful works to the children of men!  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, and praise him in the assembly of the elders.  
<span class="verse-number">33&ensp;</span>¶ He turneth rivers into a wilderness, and the watersprings into dry ground;  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, and dry ground into watersprings.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, that they may prepare a city for habitation;  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, which may yield fruits of increase.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; and suffereth not their cattle to decrease.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>Again, they are minished and brought low through oppression, affliction, and sorrow.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>He poureth contempt upon princes, and causeth them to wander in the wilderness, _where there is_ no way.  
<span class="verse-number">41&ensp;</span>Yet setteth he the poor on high from affliction, and maketh _him_ families like a flock.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>The righteous shall see _it_, and rejoice: and all iniquity shall stop her mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>Whoso _is_ wise, and will observe these _things_, even they shall understand the lovingkindness of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 108.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song <em>or</em> Psalm of David.</div>

O God, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with my glory.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Awake, psaltery and harp: I _myself_ will awake early.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>I will praise thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, among the people: and I will sing praises unto thee among the nations.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For thy mercy _is_ great above the heavens: and thy truth _reacheth_ unto the clouds.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above all the earth;  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ That thy beloved may be delivered: save _with_ thy right hand, and answer me.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Gilead _is_ mine; Manasseh _is_ mine; Ephraim also _is_ the strength of mine head; Judah _is_ my lawgiver;  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Moab _is_ my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe; over Philistia will I triumph.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>_Wilt_ not _thou_, O God, _who_ hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our hosts?  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Give us help from trouble: for vain _is_ the help of man.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Through God we shall do valiantly: for he _it is that_ shall tread down our enemies.  

## PSALM 109.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise;  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying tongue.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>They compassed me about also with words of hatred; and fought against me without a cause.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For my love they are my adversaries: but I _give myself unto_ prayer.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Set thou a wicked man over him: and let Satan stand at his right hand.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: and let his prayer become sin.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Let his days be few; _and_ let another take his office.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: let them seek _their bread_ also out of their desolate places.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; and let the strangers spoil his labour.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Let there be none to extend mercy unto him: neither let there be any to favour his fatherless children.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Let his posterity be cut off; _and_ in the generation following let their name be blotted out.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Let them be before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> continually, that he may cut off the memory of them from the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Because that he remembered not to shew mercy, but persecuted the poor and needy man, that he might even slay the broken in heart.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>As he loved cursing, so let it come unto him: as he delighted not in blessing, so let it be far from him.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, so let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Let it be unto him as the garment _which_ covereth him, and for a girdle wherewith he is girded continually.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>_Let_ this _be_ the reward of mine adversaries from the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and of them that speak evil against my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>¶ But do thou for me, O <span class="small-caps">God</span> the Lord, for thy name’s sake: because thy mercy _is_ good, deliver thou me.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>For I _am_ poor and needy, and my heart is wounded within me.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and down as the locust.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>My knees are weak through fasting; and my flesh faileth of fatness.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>I became also a reproach unto them: _when_ they looked upon me they shaked their heads.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>Help me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my God: O save me according to thy mercy:  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>That they may know that this _is_ thy hand; _that_ thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, hast done it.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>Let them curse, but bless thou: when they arise, let them be ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>Let mine adversaries be clothed with shame, and let them cover themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>I will greatly praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with my mouth; yea, I will praise him among the multitude.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>For he shall stand at the right hand of the poor, to save _him_ from those that condemn his soul.  

## PSALM 110.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> said unto my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I make thine enemies thy footstool.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: rule thou in the midst of thine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thy people _shall be_ willing in the day of thy power, in the beauties of holiness from the womb of the morning: thou hast the dew of thy youth.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou _art_ a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ The Lord at thy right hand shall strike through kings in the day of his wrath.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He shall judge among the heathen, he shall fill _the places_ with the dead bodies; he shall wound the heads over many countries.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He shall drink of the brook in the way: therefore shall he lift up the head.  

## PSALM 111.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. I will praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with _my_ whole heart, in the assembly of the upright, and _in_ the congregation.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The works of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _are_ great, sought out of all them that have pleasure therein.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>His work _is_ honourable and glorious: and his righteousness endureth for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ gracious and full of compassion.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>He hath given meat unto them that fear him: he will ever be mindful of his covenant.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ He hath shewed his people the power of his works, that he may give them the heritage of the heathen.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The works of his hands _are_ verity and judgment; all his commandments _are_ sure.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They stand fast for ever and ever, _and are_ done in truth and uprightness.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He sent redemption unto his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever: holy and reverend _is_ his name.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The fear of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ the beginning of wisdom: a good understanding have all they that do _his commandments_: his praise endureth for ever.  

## PSALM 112.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Blessed _is_ the man _that_ feareth the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _that_ delighteth greatly in his commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the upright shall be blessed.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Wealth and riches _shall be_ in his house: and his righteousness endureth for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness: _he is_ gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>A good man sheweth favour, and lendeth: he will guide his affairs with discretion.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Surely he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: his heart is fixed, trusting in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>His heart _is_ established, he shall not be afraid, until he see _his desire_ upon his enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; his righteousness endureth for ever; his horn shall be exalted with honour.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The wicked shall see _it_, and be grieved; he shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked shall perish.  

## PSALM 113.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Praise, O ye servants of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, praise the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Blessed be the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> from this time forth and for evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span> name _is_ to be praised.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ high above all nations, _and_ his glory above the heavens.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Who _is_ like unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God, who dwelleth on high,  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Who humbleth _himself_ to behold _the things that are_ in heaven, and in the earth!  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He raiseth up the poor out of the dust, _and_ lifteth the needy out of the dunghill;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>That he may set _him_ with princes, _even_ with the princes of his people.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He maketh the barren woman to keep house, _and to be_ a joyful mother of children. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 114.

When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of strange language;  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Judah was his sanctuary, _and_ Israel his dominion.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The sea saw _it_, and fled: Jordan was driven back.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The mountains skipped like rams, _and_ the little hills like lambs.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>What _ailed_ thee, O thou sea, that thou fleddest? thou Jordan, _that_ thou wast driven back?  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Ye mountains, _that_ ye skipped like rams; _and_ ye little hills, like lambs?  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Which turned the rock _into_ a standing water, the flint into a fountain of waters.  

## PSALM 115.

Not unto us, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, not unto us, but unto thy name give glory, for thy mercy, _and_ for thy truth’s sake.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Wherefore should the heathen say, Where _is_ now their God?  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>But our God _is_ in the heavens: he hath done whatsoever he hath pleased.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Their idols _are_ silver and gold, the work of men’s hands.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They have mouths, but they speak not: eyes have they, but they see not:  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>They have ears, but they hear not: noses have they, but they smell not:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>They have hands, but they handle not: feet have they, but they walk not: neither speak they through their throat.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>They that make them are like unto them; _so is_ every one that trusteth in them.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ O Israel, trust thou in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: he _is_ their help and their shield.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>O house of Aaron, trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: he _is_ their help and their shield.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Ye that fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: he _is_ their help and their shield.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath been mindful of us: he will bless _us_; he will bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>He will bless them that fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _both_ small and great.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall increase you more and more, you and your children.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Ye _are_ blessed of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> which made heaven and earth.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The heaven, _even_ the heavens, _are_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span>: but the earth hath he given to the children of men.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The dead praise not the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, neither any that go down into silence.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>But we will bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> from this time forth and for evermore. Praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 116.

I love the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, because he hath heard my voice _and_ my supplications.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Because he hath inclined his ear unto me, therefore will I call upon _him_ as long as I live.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The sorrows of death compassed me, and the pains of hell gat hold upon me: I found trouble and sorrow.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Then called I upon the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, I beseech thee, deliver my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Gracious _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and righteous; yea, our God _is_ merciful.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped me.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Return unto thy rest, O my soul; for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath dealt bountifully with thee.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>For thou hast delivered my soul from death, mine eyes from tears, _and_ my feet from falling.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>I will walk before the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in the land of the living.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ I believed, therefore have I spoken: I was greatly afflicted:  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>I said in my haste, All men _are_ liars.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>What shall I render unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _for_ all his benefits toward me?  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>I will take the cup of salvation, and call upon the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>I will pay my vows unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> now in the presence of all his people.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Precious in the sight of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ the death of his saints.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, truly I _am_ thy servant; I _am_ thy servant, _and_ the son of thine handmaid: thou hast loosed my bonds.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and will call upon the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>I will pay my vows unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> now in the presence of all his people,  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>In the courts of the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span> house, in the midst of thee, O Jerusalem. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 117.

O praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all ye nations: praise him, all ye people.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For his merciful kindness is great toward us: and the truth of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _endureth_ for ever. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 118.

O give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for _he is_ good: because his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let Israel now say, that his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Let them now that fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> say, that his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I called upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> in distress: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> answered me, _and set me_ in a large place.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ on my side; I will not fear: what can man do unto me?  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> taketh my part with them that help me: therefore shall I see _my desire_ upon them that hate me.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>_It is_ better to trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> than to put confidence in man.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>_It is_ better to trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> than to put confidence in princes.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>All nations compassed me about: but in the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will I destroy them.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>They compassed me about; yea, they compassed me about: but in the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> I will destroy them.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>They compassed me about like bees; they are quenched as the fire of thorns: for in the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> I will destroy them.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thou hast thrust sore at me that I might fall: but the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> helped me.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ my strength and song, and is become my salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>The voice of rejoicing and salvation _is_ in the tabernacles of the righteous: the right hand of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> doeth valiantly.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>The right hand of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> is exalted: the right hand of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> doeth valiantly.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath chastened me sore: but he hath not given me over unto death.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>¶ Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will go into them, _and_ I will praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>:  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>This gate of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, into which the righteous shall enter.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>The stone _which_ the builders refused is become the head _stone_ of the corner.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>This is the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span> doing; it _is_ marvellous in our eyes.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>This _is_ the day _which_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath made; we will rejoice and be glad in it.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Save now, I beseech thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, I beseech thee, send now prosperity.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>Blessed _be_ he that cometh in the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: we have blessed you out of the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>God _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, which hath shewed us light: bind the sacrifice with cords, _even_ unto the horns of the altar.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>Thou _art_ my God, and I will praise thee: _thou art_ my God, I will exalt thee.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>O give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for _he is_ good: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  

## PSALM 119.

#### <bdi dir="ltr">א ALEPH.</bdi>

Blessed _are_ the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Blessed _are_ they that keep his testimonies, _and that_ seek him with the whole heart.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>They also do no iniquity: they walk in his ways.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ Thou hast commanded _us_ to keep thy precepts diligently.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>O that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes!  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect unto all thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned thy righteous judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ב BETH.</bdi>

Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his way? by taking heed _thereto_ according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander from thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Thy word have I hid in mine heart, that I might not sin against thee.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Blessed _art_ thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: teach me thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>¶ With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as _much as_ in all riches.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>I will meditate in thy precepts, and have respect unto thy ways.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy word.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ג GIMEL.</bdi>

Deal bountifully with thy servant, _that_ I may live, and keep thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>Open thou mine eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>I _am_ a stranger in the earth: hide not thy commandments from me.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>My soul breaketh for the longing _that it hath_ unto thy judgments at all times.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Thou hast rebuked the proud _that are_ cursed, which do err from thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>Remove from me reproach and contempt; for I have kept thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Princes also did sit _and_ speak against me: _but_ thy servant did meditate in thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>Thy testimonies also _are_ my delight _and_ my counsellors.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ד DALETH.</bdi>

My soul cleaveth unto the dust: quicken thou me according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>¶ I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: teach me thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">27&ensp;</span>Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: so shall I talk of thy wondrous works.  
<span class="verse-number">28&ensp;</span>¶ My soul melteth for heaviness: strengthen thou me according unto thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">29&ensp;</span>Remove from me the way of lying: and grant me thy law graciously.  
<span class="verse-number">30&ensp;</span>¶ I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments have I laid _before me_.  
<span class="verse-number">31&ensp;</span>I have stuck unto thy testimonies: O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, put me not to shame.  
<span class="verse-number">32&ensp;</span>I will run the way of thy commandments, when thou shalt enlarge my heart.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ה HE.</bdi>

Teach me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, the way of thy statutes; and I shall keep it _unto_ the end.  
<span class="verse-number">34&ensp;</span>Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; yea, I shall observe it with _my_ whole heart.  
<span class="verse-number">35&ensp;</span>¶ Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; for therein do I delight.  
<span class="verse-number">36&ensp;</span>Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, and not to covetousness.  
<span class="verse-number">37&ensp;</span>Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; _and_ quicken thou me in thy way.  
<span class="verse-number">38&ensp;</span>Stablish thy word unto thy servant, who _is devoted_ to thy fear.  
<span class="verse-number">39&ensp;</span>Turn away my reproach which I fear: for thy judgments _are_ good.  
<span class="verse-number">40&ensp;</span>Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy righteousness.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ו VAU.</bdi>

Let thy mercies come also unto me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _even_ thy salvation, according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">42&ensp;</span>So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth me: for I trust in thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">43&ensp;</span>¶ And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; for I have hoped in thy judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">44&ensp;</span>So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever.  
<span class="verse-number">45&ensp;</span>¶ And I will walk at liberty: for I seek thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">46&ensp;</span>I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, and will not be ashamed.  
<span class="verse-number">47&ensp;</span>And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I have loved.  
<span class="verse-number">48&ensp;</span>My hands also will I lift up unto thy commandments, which I have loved; and I will meditate in thy statutes.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ז ZAIN.</bdi>

Remember the word unto thy servant, upon which thou hast caused me to hope.  
<span class="verse-number">50&ensp;</span>This _is_ my comfort in my affliction: for thy word hath quickened me.  
<span class="verse-number">51&ensp;</span>The proud have had me greatly in derision: _yet_ have I not declined from thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">52&ensp;</span>I remembered thy judgments of old, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and have comforted myself.  
<span class="verse-number">53&ensp;</span>Horror hath taken hold upon me because of the wicked that forsake thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">54&ensp;</span>Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my pilgrimage.  
<span class="verse-number">55&ensp;</span>¶ I have remembered thy name, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, in the night, and have kept thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">56&ensp;</span>This I had, because I kept thy precepts.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ח CHETH.</bdi>

_Thou art_ my portion, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: I have said that I would keep thy words.  
<span class="verse-number">58&ensp;</span>I intreated thy favour with _my_ whole heart: be merciful unto me according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">59&ensp;</span>¶ I thought on my ways, and turned my feet unto thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">60&ensp;</span>I made haste, and delayed not to keep thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">61&ensp;</span>The bands of the wicked have robbed me: _but_ I have not forgotten thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">62&ensp;</span>At midnight I will rise to give thanks unto thee because of thy righteous judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">63&ensp;</span>I _am_ a companion of all _them_ that fear thee, and of them that keep thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">64&ensp;</span>The earth, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy statutes.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ט TETH.</bdi>

Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, according unto thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">66&ensp;</span>Teach me good judgment and knowledge: for I have believed thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">67&ensp;</span>Before I was afflicted I went astray: but now have I kept thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">68&ensp;</span>Thou _art_ good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">69&ensp;</span>¶ The proud have forged a lie against me: _but_ I will keep thy precepts with _my_ whole heart.  
<span class="verse-number">70&ensp;</span>Their heart is as fat as grease; _but_ I delight in thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">71&ensp;</span>_It is_ good for me that I have been afflicted; that I might learn thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">72&ensp;</span>The law of thy mouth _is_ better unto me than thousands of gold and silver.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">י JOD.</bdi>

Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me understanding, that I may learn thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">74&ensp;</span>They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; because I have hoped in thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">75&ensp;</span>I know, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, that thy judgments _are_ right, and _that_ thou in faithfulness hast afflicted me.  
<span class="verse-number">76&ensp;</span>¶ Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort, according to thy word unto thy servant.  
<span class="verse-number">77&ensp;</span>Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live: for thy law _is_ my delight.  
<span class="verse-number">78&ensp;</span>¶ Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me without a cause: _but_ I will meditate in thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">79&ensp;</span>Let those that fear thee turn unto me, and those that have known thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">80&ensp;</span>Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; that I be not ashamed.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">כ CAPH.</bdi>

My soul fainteth for thy salvation: _but_ I hope in thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">82&ensp;</span>Mine eyes fail for thy word, saying, When wilt thou comfort me?  
<span class="verse-number">83&ensp;</span>For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; _yet_ do I not forget thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">84&ensp;</span>How many _are_ the days of thy servant? when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me?  
<span class="verse-number">85&ensp;</span>¶ The proud have digged pits for me, which _are_ not after thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">86&ensp;</span>All thy commandments _are_ faithful: they persecute me wrongfully; help thou me.  
<span class="verse-number">87&ensp;</span>They had almost consumed me upon earth; but I forsook not thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">88&ensp;</span>Quicken me after thy lovingkindness; so shall I keep the testimony of thy mouth.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ל LAMED.</bdi>

For ever, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thy word is settled in heaven.  
<span class="verse-number">90&ensp;</span>Thy faithfulness _is_ unto all generations: thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.  
<span class="verse-number">91&ensp;</span>They continue this day according to thine ordinances: for all _are_ thy servants.  
<span class="verse-number">92&ensp;</span>Unless thy law _had been_ my delights, I should then have perished in mine affliction.  
<span class="verse-number">93&ensp;</span>I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast quickened me.  
<span class="verse-number">94&ensp;</span>I _am_ thine, save me; for I have sought thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">95&ensp;</span>The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: _but_ I will consider thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">96&ensp;</span>I have seen an end of all perfection: _but_ thy commandment _is_ exceeding broad.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">מ MEM.</bdi>

O how love I thy law! it _is_ my meditation all the day.  
<span class="verse-number">98&ensp;</span>¶ Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than mine enemies: for they _are_ ever with me.  
<span class="verse-number">99&ensp;</span>I have more understanding than all my teachers: for thy testimonies _are_ my meditation.  
<span class="verse-number">100&ensp;</span>I understand more than the ancients, because I keep thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">101&ensp;</span>I have refrained my feet from every evil way, that I might keep thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">102&ensp;</span>I have not departed from thy judgments: for thou hast taught me.  
<span class="verse-number">103&ensp;</span>¶ How sweet are thy words unto my taste! _yea, sweeter_ than honey to my mouth!  
<span class="verse-number">104&ensp;</span>Through thy precepts I get understanding: therefore I hate every false way.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">נ NUN.</bdi>

Thy word _is_ a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto my path.  
<span class="verse-number">106&ensp;</span>I have sworn, and I will perform _it_, that I will keep thy righteous judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">107&ensp;</span>I am afflicted very much: quicken me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, according unto thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">108&ensp;</span>Accept, I beseech thee, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and teach me thy judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">109&ensp;</span>¶ My soul _is_ continually in my hand: yet do I not forget thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">110&ensp;</span>The wicked have laid a snare for me: yet I erred not from thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">111&ensp;</span>¶ Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: for they _are_ the rejoicing of my heart.  
<span class="verse-number">112&ensp;</span>I have inclined mine heart to perform thy statutes alway, _even unto_ the end.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ס SAMECH.</bdi>

I hate _vain_ thoughts: but thy law do I love.  
<span class="verse-number">114&ensp;</span>Thou _art_ my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">115&ensp;</span>Depart from me, ye evildoers: for I will keep the commandments of my God.  
<span class="verse-number">116&ensp;</span>¶ Uphold me according unto thy word, that I may live: and let me not be ashamed of my hope.  
<span class="verse-number">117&ensp;</span>Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe: and I will have respect unto thy statutes continually.  
<span class="verse-number">118&ensp;</span>¶ Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes: for their deceit _is_ falsehood.  
<span class="verse-number">119&ensp;</span>Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth _like_ dross: therefore I love thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">120&ensp;</span>My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of thy judgments.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ע AIN.</bdi>

I have done judgment and justice: leave me not to mine oppressors.  
<span class="verse-number">122&ensp;</span>Be surety for thy servant for good: let not the proud oppress me.  
<span class="verse-number">123&ensp;</span>Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the word of thy righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">124&ensp;</span>¶ Deal with thy servant according unto thy mercy, and teach me thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">125&ensp;</span>I _am_ thy servant; give me understanding, that I may know thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">126&ensp;</span>_It is_ time for _thee_, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, to work: _for_ they have made void thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">127&ensp;</span>¶ Therefore I love thy commandments above gold; yea, above fine gold.  
<span class="verse-number">128&ensp;</span>Therefore I esteem all _thy_ precepts _concerning_ all _things to be_ right; _and_ I hate every false way.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">פ PE.</bdi>

Thy testimonies _are_ wonderful: therefore doth my soul keep them.  
<span class="verse-number">130&ensp;</span>The entrance of thy words giveth light; it giveth understanding unto the simple.  
<span class="verse-number">131&ensp;</span>I opened my mouth, and panted: for I longed for thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">132&ensp;</span>Look thou upon me, and be merciful unto me, as thou usest to do unto those that love thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">133&ensp;</span>Order my steps in thy word: and let not any iniquity have dominion over me.  
<span class="verse-number">134&ensp;</span>Deliver me from the oppression of man: so will I keep thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">135&ensp;</span>Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; and teach me thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">136&ensp;</span>Rivers of waters run down mine eyes, because they keep not thy law.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">צ TZADDI.</bdi>

Righteous _art_ thou, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and upright _are_ thy judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">138&ensp;</span>Thy testimonies _that_ thou hast commanded _are_ righteous and very faithful.  
<span class="verse-number">139&ensp;</span>My zeal hath consumed me, because mine enemies have forgotten thy words.  
<span class="verse-number">140&ensp;</span>Thy word _is_ very pure: therefore thy servant loveth it.  
<span class="verse-number">141&ensp;</span>I _am_ small and despised: _yet_ do not I forget thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">142&ensp;</span>Thy righteousness _is_ an everlasting righteousness, and thy law _is_ the truth.  
<span class="verse-number">143&ensp;</span>¶ Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: _yet_ thy commandments _are_ my delights.  
<span class="verse-number">144&ensp;</span>The righteousness of thy testimonies _is_ everlasting: give me understanding, and I shall live.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ק KOPH.</bdi>

I cried with _my_ whole heart; hear me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: I will keep thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">146&ensp;</span>I cried unto thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">147&ensp;</span>¶ I prevented the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">148&ensp;</span>Mine eyes prevent the _night_ watches, that I might meditate in thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">149&ensp;</span>Hear my voice according unto thy lovingkindness: O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, quicken me according to thy judgment.  
<span class="verse-number">150&ensp;</span>¶ They draw nigh that follow after mischief: they are far from thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">151&ensp;</span>Thou _art_ near, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and all thy commandments _are_ truth.  
<span class="verse-number">152&ensp;</span>Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast founded them for ever.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ר RESH.</bdi>

Consider mine affliction, and deliver me: for I do not forget thy law.  
<span class="verse-number">154&ensp;</span>Plead my cause, and deliver me: quicken me according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">155&ensp;</span>Salvation _is_ far from the wicked: for they seek not thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">156&ensp;</span>Great _are_ thy tender mercies, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: quicken me according to thy judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">157&ensp;</span>Many _are_ my persecutors and mine enemies; _yet_ do I not decline from thy testimonies.  
<span class="verse-number">158&ensp;</span>I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; because they kept not thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">159&ensp;</span>Consider how I love thy precepts: quicken me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, according to thy lovingkindness.  
<span class="verse-number">160&ensp;</span>Thy word _is_ true _from_ the beginning: and every one of thy righteous judgments _endureth_ for ever.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ש SCHIN.</bdi>

Princes have persecuted me without a cause: but my heart standeth in awe of thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">162&ensp;</span>I rejoice at thy word, as one that findeth great spoil.  
<span class="verse-number">163&ensp;</span>I hate and abhor lying: _but_ thy law do I love.  
<span class="verse-number">164&ensp;</span>Seven times a day do I praise thee because of thy righteous judgments.  
<span class="verse-number">165&ensp;</span>Great peace have they which love thy law: and nothing shall offend them.  
<span class="verse-number">166&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, I have hoped for thy salvation, and done thy commandments.  
<span class="verse-number">167&ensp;</span>¶ My soul hath kept thy testimonies; and I love them exceedingly.  
<span class="verse-number">168&ensp;</span>I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: for all my ways _are_ before thee.  

#### <bdi dir="ltr">ת TAU.</bdi>

Let my cry come near before thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: give me understanding according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">170&ensp;</span>Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me according to thy word.  
<span class="verse-number">171&ensp;</span>My lips shall utter praise, when thou hast taught me thy statutes.  
<span class="verse-number">172&ensp;</span>My tongue shall speak of thy word: for all thy commandments _are_ righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">173&ensp;</span>¶ Let thine hand help me; for I have chosen thy precepts.  
<span class="verse-number">174&ensp;</span>I have longed for thy salvation, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and thy law _is_ my delight.  
<span class="verse-number">175&ensp;</span>Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy judgments help me.  
<span class="verse-number">176&ensp;</span>I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; for I do not forget thy commandments.  

## PSALM 120.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

In my distress I cried unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and he heard me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Deliver my soul, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, from lying lips, _and_ from a deceitful tongue.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee, thou false tongue?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, _that_ I dwell in the tents of Kedar!  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>I _am for_ peace: but when I speak, they _are_ for war.  

## PSALM 121.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>My help _cometh_ from the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, which made heaven and earth.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ thy keeper: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ thy shade upon thy right hand.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve thy soul.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for evermore.  

## PSALM 122.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees of David.</div>

I was glad when they said unto me, Let us go into the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Jerusalem is builded as a city that is compact together:  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, unto the testimony of Israel, to give thanks unto the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>For there are set thrones of judgment, the thrones of the house of David.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that love thee.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Peace be within thy walls, _and_ prosperity within thy palaces.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>For my brethren and companions’ sakes, I will now say, Peace _be_ within thee.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Because of the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God I will seek thy good.  

## PSALM 123.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

Unto thee lift I up mine eyes, O thou that dwellest in the heavens.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Behold, as the eyes of servants _look_ unto the hand of their masters, _and_ as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her mistress; so our eyes _wait_ upon the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> our God, until that he have mercy upon us.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Have mercy upon us, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, have mercy upon us: for we are exceedingly filled with contempt.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that are at ease, _and_ with the contempt of the proud.  

## PSALM 124.
