<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees of David.</div>

If _it had not been_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> who was on our side, now may Israel say;  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>If _it had not been_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> who was on our side, when men rose up against us:  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Then they had swallowed us up quick, when their wrath was kindled against us:  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Then the waters had overwhelmed us, the stream had gone over our soul:  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Then the proud waters had gone over our soul.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, who hath not given us _as_ a prey to their teeth.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Our soul is escaped as a bird out of the snare of the fowlers: the snare is broken, and we are escaped.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Our help _is_ in the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, who made heaven and earth.  

## PSALM 125.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

They that trust in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _shall be_ as mount Zion, _which_ cannot be removed, _but_ abideth for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>As the mountains _are_ round about Jerusalem, so the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ round about his people from henceforth even for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands unto iniquity.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ Do good, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, unto _those that be_ good, and _to them that are_ upright in their hearts.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>As for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways, the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: _but_ peace _shall be_ upon Israel.  

## PSALM 126.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

When the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> turned again the captivity of Zion, we were like them that dream.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue with singing: then said they among the heathen, The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath done great things for them.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath done great things for us; _whereof_ we are glad.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ Turn again our captivity, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, as the streams in the south.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>They that sow in tears shall reap in joy.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, shall doubtless come again with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves _with him_.  

## PSALM 127.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees for Solomon.</div>

Except the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> build the house, they labour in vain that build it: except the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> keep the city, the watchman waketh _but_ in vain.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>_It is_ vain for you to rise up early, to sit up late, to eat the bread of sorrows: _for_ so he giveth his beloved sleep.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Lo, children _are_ an heritage of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: _and_ the fruit of the womb _is his_ reward.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>As arrows _are_ in the hand of a mighty man; so _are_ children of the youth.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Happy _is_ the man that hath his quiver full of them: they shall not be ashamed, but they shall speak with the enemies in the gate.  

## PSALM 128.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

Blessed _is_ every one that feareth the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; that walketh in his ways.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>For thou shalt eat the labour of thine hands: happy _shalt_ thou _be_, and _it shall be_ well with thee.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thy wife _shall be_ as a fruitful vine by the sides of thine house: thy children like olive plants round about thy table.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Behold, that thus shall the man be blessed that feareth the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall bless thee out of Zion: and thou shalt see the good of Jerusalem all the days of thy life.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Yea, thou shalt see thy children’s children, _and_ peace upon Israel.  

## PSALM 129.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth, may Israel now say:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Many a time have they afflicted me from my youth: yet they have not prevailed against me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The plowers plowed upon my back: they made long their furrows.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ righteous: he hath cut asunder the cords of the wicked.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ Let them all be confounded and turned back that hate Zion.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Let them be as the grass _upon_ the housetops, which withereth afore it groweth up:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Wherewith the mower filleth not his hand; nor he that bindeth sheaves his bosom.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Neither do they which go by say, The blessing of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _be_ upon you: we bless you in the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 130.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

Out of the depths have I cried unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Lord, hear my voice: let thine ears be attentive to the voice of my supplications.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>If thou, <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, shouldest mark iniquities, O Lord, who shall stand?  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>But _there is_ forgiveness with thee, that thou mayest be feared.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ I wait for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, my soul doth wait, and in his word do I hope.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>My soul _waiteth_ for the Lord more than they that watch for the morning: _I say, more than_ they that watch for the morning.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Let Israel hope in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for with the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _there is_ mercy, and with him _is_ plenteous redemption.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>And he shall redeem Israel from all his iniquities.  

## PSALM 131.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees of David.</div>

<span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, my heart is not haughty, nor mine eyes lofty: neither do I exercise myself in great matters, or in things too high for me.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Surely I have behaved and quieted myself, as a child that is weaned of his mother: my soul _is_ even as a weaned child.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let Israel hope in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> from henceforth and for ever.  

## PSALM 132.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

<span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, remember David, _and_ all his afflictions:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>How he sware unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _and_ vowed unto the mighty _God_ of Jacob;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Surely I will not come into the tabernacle of my house, nor go up into my bed;  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>I will not give sleep to mine eyes, _or_ slumber to mine eyelids,  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Until I find out a place for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, an habitation for the mighty _God_ of Jacob.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Lo, we heard of it at Ephratah: we found it in the fields of the wood.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>We will go into his tabernacles: we will worship at his footstool.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Arise, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, into thy rest; thou, and the ark of thy strength.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness; and let thy saints shout for joy.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>For thy servant David’s sake turn not away the face of thine anointed.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>¶ The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath sworn _in_ truth unto David; he will not turn from it; Of the fruit of thy body will I set upon thy throne.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>If thy children will keep my covenant and my testimony that I shall teach them, their children shall also sit upon thy throne for evermore.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath chosen Zion; he hath desired _it_ for his habitation.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>This _is_ my rest for ever: here will I dwell; for I have desired it.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>I will abundantly bless her provision: I will satisfy her poor with bread.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>I will also clothe her priests with salvation: and her saints shall shout aloud for joy.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>There will I make the horn of David to bud: I have ordained a lamp for mine anointed.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>His enemies will I clothe with shame: but upon himself shall his crown flourish.  

## PSALM 133.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees of David.</div>

Behold, how good and how pleasant _it is_ for brethren to dwell together in unity!  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>_It is_ like the precious ointment upon the head, that ran down upon the beard, _even_ Aaron’s beard: that went down to the skirts of his garments;  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>As the dew of Hermon, _and as the dew_ that descended upon the mountains of Zion: for there the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> commanded the blessing, _even_ life for evermore.  

## PSALM 134.

<div class="psalm-title">A Song of degrees.</div>

Behold, bless ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, all _ye_ servants of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, which by night stand in the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Lift up your hands _in_ the sanctuary, and bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> that made heaven and earth bless thee out of Zion.  

## PSALM 135.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Praise ye the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; praise _him_, O ye servants of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Ye that stand in the house of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, in the courts of the house of our God,  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ good: sing praises unto his name; for _it is_ pleasant.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> hath chosen Jacob unto himself, _and_ Israel for his peculiar treasure.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ For I know that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ great, and _that_ our Lord _is_ above all gods.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Whatsoever the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> pleased, _that_ did he in heaven, and in earth, in the seas, and all deep places.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>He causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth; he maketh lightnings for the rain; he bringeth the wind out of his treasuries.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Who smote the firstborn of Egypt, both of man and beast.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>_Who_ sent tokens and wonders into the midst of thee, O Egypt, upon Pharaoh, and upon all his servants.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Who smote great nations, and slew mighty kings;  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, and all the kingdoms of Canaan:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>And gave their land _for_ an heritage, an heritage unto Israel his people.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thy name, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _endureth_ for ever; _and_ thy memorial, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, throughout all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will judge his people, and he will repent himself concerning his servants.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>¶ The idols of the heathen _are_ silver and gold, the work of men’s hands.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>They have mouths, but they speak not; eyes have they, but they see not;  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>They have ears, but they hear not; neither is there _any_ breath in their mouths.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>They that make them are like unto them: _so is_ every one that trusteth in them.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O house of Israel: bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O house of Aaron:  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>Bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O house of Levi: ye that fear the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, bless the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Blessed be the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> out of Zion, which dwelleth at Jerusalem. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 136.

O give thanks unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; for _he is_ good: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>O give thanks unto the God of gods: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>O give thanks to the Lord of lords: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>To him who alone doeth great wonders: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>To him that by wisdom made the heavens: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>To him that stretched out the earth above the waters: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>To him that made great lights: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The sun to rule by day: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The moon and stars to rule by night: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ To him that smote Egypt in their firstborn: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>And brought out Israel from among them: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>With a strong hand, and with a stretched out arm: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>To him which divided the Red sea into parts: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>And made Israel to pass through the midst of it: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>But overthrew Pharaoh and his host in the Red sea: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>To him which led his people through the wilderness: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>To him which smote great kings: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>And slew famous kings: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Sihon king of the Amorites: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>And Og the king of Bashan: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>And gave their land for an heritage: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>_Even_ an heritage unto Israel his servant: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>¶ Who remembered us in our low estate: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>And hath redeemed us from our enemies: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">25&ensp;</span>Who giveth food to all flesh: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  
<span class="verse-number">26&ensp;</span>O give thanks unto the God of heaven: for his mercy _endureth_ for ever.  

## PSALM 137.

By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, yea, we wept, when we remembered Zion.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>We hanged our harps upon the willows in the midst thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For there they that carried us away captive required of us a song; and they that wasted us _required of us_ mirth, _saying_, Sing us _one_ of the songs of Zion.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>How shall we sing the <span class="small-caps">Lord’s</span> song in a strange land?  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand forget _her cunning_.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to the roof of my mouth; if I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Remember, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem; who said, Rase _it_, rase _it, even_ to the foundation thereof.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>O daughter of Babylon, who art to be destroyed; happy _shall he be_, that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Happy _shall he be_, that taketh and dasheth thy little ones against the stones.  

## PSALM 138.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

I will praise thee with my whole heart: before the gods will I sing praise unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I will worship toward thy holy temple, and praise thy name for thy lovingkindness and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy word above all thy name.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>In the day when I cried thou answeredst me, _and_ strengthenedst me _with_ strength in my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>All the kings of the earth shall praise thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, when they hear the words of thy mouth.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Yea, they shall sing in the ways of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for great _is_ the glory of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ Though the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _be_ high, yet hath he respect unto the lowly: but the proud he knoweth afar off.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me: thou shalt stretch forth thine hand against the wrath of mine enemies, and thy right hand shall save me.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will perfect _that which_ concerneth me: thy mercy, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, _endureth_ for ever: forsake not the works of thine own hands.  

## PSALM 139.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou hast searched me, and known _me_.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Thou knowest my downsitting and mine uprising, thou understandest my thought afar off.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Thou compassest my path and my lying down, and art acquainted _with_ all my ways.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For _there is_ not a word in my tongue, _but_, lo, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, thou knowest it altogether.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thine hand upon me.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>_Such_ knowledge _is_ too wonderful for me; it is high, I cannot _attain_ unto it.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy presence?  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>If I ascend up into heaven, thou _art_ there: if I make my bed in hell, behold, thou _art there_.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>_If_ I take the wings of the morning, _and_ dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea;  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand shall hold me.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; even the night shall be light about me.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Yea, the darkness hideth not from thee; but the night shineth as the day: the darkness and the light _are_ both alike _to thee_.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast covered me in my mother’s womb.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>I will praise thee; for I am fearfully _and_ wonderfully made: marvellous _are_ thy works; and _that_ my soul knoweth right well.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>My substance was not hid from thee, when I was made in secret, _and_ curiously wrought in the lowest parts of the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Thine eyes did see my substance, yet being unperfect; and in thy book all _my members_ were written, _which_ in continuance were fashioned, when _as yet there was_ none of them.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>¶ How precious also are thy thoughts unto me, O God! how great is the sum of them!  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>_If_ I should count them, they are more in number than the sand: when I awake, I am still with thee.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: depart from me therefore, ye bloody men.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>For they speak against thee wickedly, _and_ thine enemies take _thy name_ in vain.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>Do not I hate them, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, that hate thee? and am not I grieved with those that rise up against thee?  
<span class="verse-number">22&ensp;</span>I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them mine enemies.  
<span class="verse-number">23&ensp;</span>Search me, O God, and know my heart: try me, and know my thoughts:  
<span class="verse-number">24&ensp;</span>And see if _there be any_ wicked way in me, and lead me in the way everlasting.  

## PSALM 140.

<div class="psalm-title">To the chief Musician, A Psalm of David.</div>

Deliver me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, from the evil man: preserve me from the violent man;  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Which imagine mischiefs in _their_ heart; continually are they gathered together _for_ war.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; adders’ poison _is_ under their lips. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Keep me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, from the hands of the wicked; preserve me from the violent man; who have purposed to overthrow my goings.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; they have spread a net by the wayside; they have set gins for me. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I said unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, Thou _art_ my God: hear the voice of my supplications, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>O <span class="small-caps">God</span> the Lord, the strength of my salvation, thou hast covered my head in the day of battle.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>¶ Grant not, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, the desires of the wicked: further not his wicked device; _lest_ they exalt themselves. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>_As for_ the head of those that compass me about, let the mischief of their own lips cover them.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Let burning coals fall upon them: let them be cast into the fire; into deep pits, that they rise not up again.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Let not an evil speaker be established in the earth: evil shall hunt the violent man to overthrow _him_.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>I know that the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> will maintain the cause of the afflicted, _and_ the right of the poor.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Surely the righteous shall give thanks unto thy name: the upright shall dwell in thy presence.  

## PSALM 141.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

<span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, I cry unto thee: make haste unto me; give ear unto my voice, when I cry unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let my prayer be set forth before thee _as_ incense; _and_ the lifting up of my hands _as_ the evening sacrifice.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Set a watch, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, before my mouth; keep the door of my lips.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Incline not my heart to _any_ evil thing, to practise wicked works with men that work iniquity: and let me not eat of their dainties.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ Let the righteous smite me; _it shall be_ a kindness: and let him reprove me; _it shall be_ an excellent oil, _which_ shall not break my head: for yet my prayer also _shall be_ in their calamities.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>When their judges are overthrown in stony places, they shall hear my words; for they are sweet.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Our bones are scattered at the grave’s mouth, as when one cutteth and cleaveth _wood_ upon the earth.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>But mine eyes _are_ unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">God</span> the Lord: in thee is my trust; leave not my soul destitute.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Keep me from the snares _which_ they have laid for me, and the gins of the workers of iniquity.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Let the wicked fall into their own nets, whilst that I withal escape.  

## PSALM 142.

<div class="psalm-title">Maschil of David; A Prayer when he was in the cave.</div>

I cried unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with my voice; with my voice unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> did I make my supplication.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>I poured out my complaint before him; I shewed before him my trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then thou knewest my path. In the way wherein I walked have they privily laid a snare for me.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>¶ I looked on _my_ right hand, and beheld, but _there was_ no man that would know me: refuge failed me; no man cared for my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I cried unto thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: I said, Thou _art_ my refuge _and_ my portion in the land of the living.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Attend unto my cry; for I am brought very low: deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger than I.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the righteous shall compass me about; for thou shalt deal bountifully with me.  

## PSALM 143.

<div class="psalm-title">A Psalm of David.</div>

Hear my prayer, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, give ear to my supplications: in thy faithfulness answer me, _and_ in thy righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight shall no man living be justified.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; he hath smitten my life down to the ground; he hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those that have been long dead.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; my heart within me is desolate.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I remember the days of old; I meditate on all thy works; I muse on the work of thy hands.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>I stretch forth my hands unto thee: my soul _thirsteth_ after thee, as a thirsty land. Selah.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Hear me speedily, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: my spirit faileth: hide not thy face from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Cause me to hear thy lovingkindness in the morning; for in thee do I trust: cause me to know the way wherein I should walk; for I lift up my soul unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Deliver me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, from mine enemies: I flee unto thee to hide me.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Teach me to do thy will; for thou _art_ my God: thy spirit _is_ good; lead me into the land of uprightness.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Quicken me, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, for thy name’s sake: for thy righteousness’ sake bring my soul out of trouble.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>And of thy mercy cut off mine enemies, and destroy all them that afflict my soul: for I _am_ thy servant.  

## PSALM 144.

<div class="psalm-title"><em>A Psalm</em> of David.</div>

Blessed _be_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> my strength, which teacheth my hands to war, _and_ my fingers to fight:  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>My goodness, and my fortress; my high tower, and my deliverer; my shield, and _he_ in whom I trust; who subdueth my people under me.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span><span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, what _is_ man, that thou takest knowledge of him! _or_ the son of man, that thou makest account of him!  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Man is like to vanity: his days _are_ as a shadow that passeth away.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Bow thy heavens, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and come down: touch the mountains, and they shall smoke.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Cast forth lightning, and scatter them: shoot out thine arrows, and destroy them.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Send thine hand from above; rid me, and deliver me out of great waters, from the hand of strange children;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand _is_ a right hand of falsehood.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>¶ I will sing a new song unto thee, O God: upon a psaltery _and_ an instrument of ten strings will I sing praises unto thee.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>_It is he_ that giveth salvation unto kings: who delivereth David his servant from the hurtful sword.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand _is_ a right hand of falsehood:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>That our sons _may be_ as plants grown up in their youth; _that_ our daughters _may be_ as corner stones, polished _after_ the similitude of a palace:  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>_That_ our garners _may be_ full, affording all manner of store: _that_ our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our streets:  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>_That_ our oxen _may be_ strong to labour; _that there be_ no breaking in, nor going out; that _there be_ no complaining in our streets.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>Happy _is that_ people, that is in such a case: _yea_, happy _is that_ people, whose God _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 145.

<div class="psalm-title">David’s <em>Psalm</em> of praise.</div>

I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever and ever.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever and ever.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Great _is_ the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness _is_ unsearchable.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall declare thy mighty acts.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, and of thy wondrous works.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>And _men_ shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I will declare thy greatness.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, and shall sing of thy righteousness.  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and of great mercy.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ good to all: and his tender mercies _are_ over all his works.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>¶ All thy works shall praise thee, O <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>; and thy saints shall bless thee.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy power;  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the glorious majesty of his kingdom.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Thy kingdom _is_ an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion _endureth_ throughout all generations.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all _those that be_ bowed down.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their meat in due season.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>Thou openest thine hand, and satisfiest the desire of every living thing.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his works.  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> _is_ nigh unto all them that call upon him, to all that call upon him in truth.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: he also will hear their cry, and will save them.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked will he destroy.  
<span class="verse-number">21&ensp;</span>My mouth shall speak the praise of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: and let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.  

## PSALM 146.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O my soul.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>While I live will I praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: I will sing praises unto my God while I have any being.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Put not your trust in princes, _nor_ in the son of man, in whom _there is_ no help.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very day his thoughts perish.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>¶ Happy _is he_ that _hath_ the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope _is_ in the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> his God:  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein _is_: which keepeth truth for ever:  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: which giveth food to the hungry. The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> looseth the prisoners:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> openeth _the eyes of_ the blind: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> raiseth them that are bowed down: the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> loveth the righteous:  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> shall reign for ever, _even_ thy God, O Zion, unto all generations. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 147.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for _it is_ good to sing praises unto our God; for _it is_ pleasant; _and_ praise is comely.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the outcasts of Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by _their_ names.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Great _is_ our Lord, and of great power: his understanding _is_ infinite.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the ground.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>Sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp unto our God:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains.  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>He giveth to the beast his food, _and_ to the young ravens which cry.  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man.  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>The <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that hope in his mercy.  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>¶ Praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion.  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed thy children within thee.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>He maketh peace _in_ thy borders, _and_ filleth thee with the finest of the wheat.  
<span class="verse-number">15&ensp;</span>He sendeth forth his commandment _upon_ earth: his word runneth very swiftly.  
<span class="verse-number">16&ensp;</span>He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoarfrost like ashes.  
<span class="verse-number">17&ensp;</span>He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his cold?  
<span class="verse-number">18&ensp;</span>He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind to blow, _and_ the waters flow.  
<span class="verse-number">19&ensp;</span>He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his judgments unto Israel.  
<span class="verse-number">20&ensp;</span>He hath not dealt so with any nation: and _as for his_ judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 148.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> from the heavens: praise him in the heights.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that _be_ above the heavens.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Let them praise the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for he commanded, and they were created.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass.  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>¶ Praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps:  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>Fire, and hail; snow, and vapour; stormy wind fulfilling his word:  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars:  
<span class="verse-number">10&ensp;</span>Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl:  
<span class="verse-number">11&ensp;</span>Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth:  
<span class="verse-number">12&ensp;</span>Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children:  
<span class="verse-number">13&ensp;</span>Let them praise the name of the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>: for his name alone is excellent; his glory _is_ above the earth and heaven.  
<span class="verse-number">14&ensp;</span>He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; _even_ of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 149.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Sing unto the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> a new song, _and_ his praise in the congregation of saints.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>For the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span> taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Let the saints be joyful in glory: let them sing aloud upon their beds.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>¶ _Let_ the high _praises_ of God _be_ in their mouth, and a twoedged sword in their hand;  
<span class="verse-number">7&ensp;</span>To execute vengeance upon the heathen, _and_ punishments upon the people;  
<span class="verse-number">8&ensp;</span>To bind their kings with chains, and their nobles with fetters of iron;  
<span class="verse-number">9&ensp;</span>To execute upon them the judgment written: this honour have all his saints. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.  

## PSALM 150.

Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power.  
<span class="verse-number">2&ensp;</span>Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness.  
<span class="verse-number">3&ensp;</span>Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp.  
<span class="verse-number">4&ensp;</span>Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs.  
<span class="verse-number">5&ensp;</span>Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals.  
<span class="verse-number">6&ensp;</span>Let every thing that hath breath praise the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>. Praise ye the <span class="small-caps">Lord</span>.
